# stratus code map

> **Stamped:** 2026-07-23 at commit `7e66a22`+GR.1 (shas are no longer stamped post-hoc ‚ÄĒ the amend that would write one changes it again; the parent + task id is stable, see STATE D97). **GR.1 ‚ÄĒ following ledger: schema + ingest/ratchet routes** [xhigh, no deps, **$0**] **opens the GR lane**, the last one in Wave 3. New tables `following_runs` + `following` (migration **`0019`** ‚ÄĒ the journal's first move since 0018) and a new `src/x/routes/following.ts` mounted right after `harvest`. One $0 DOM scrape of my own `/following` page yields BOTH sides (X renders a "Follows you" badge per row), so there is no API sync and no `follows.write` scope ‚ÄĒ unfollowing stays manual in the X app and this layer only ever nudges. The load-bearing rule: **presence is ground truth, absence is only evidence when the scroll finished** ‚ÄĒ batches update what they see, and only a run closed `done:true` **with `rowsSeen > 0`** reconciles (unseen `active|queued`‚Üí`gone`, unseen `done`‚Üí`confirmed`, seen `done`‚Üí`queued`). A zero-row close is stamped `completed_at` but never `complete`, so a broken selector cannot wipe the ledger. `first_seen_at` is the fill-only follow-date proxy (¬ß7.11); a `confirmed`/`gone` handle seen again revives to `active` without resetting it. Prior state, still current: `GET /x/playbook` carries `timelineFunnel: {cells, totalSeen, totalReplied}` ‚ÄĒ the ambient corpus's SECOND reader. Pure `buildTimelineFunnel` is playbook **¬ß12** (¬ß11 is AI.12's model cell); `deriveTimelineBand` recomputes the band at read time via shared `classifyBand` (¬ß7.12 ‚ÄĒ never stored) and returns `Band | 'unknown'`, where **`'unknown'` = no `tweet_time` (no age ‚áí no vpm ‚áí nothing to classify) and NEVER folds into the real `null` band** (`null` = judged not worth a reply). First sighting per tweet is the band that mattered ‚ÄĒ enforced by `min(captured_at)` + bare columns in `loadTimelineFunnel`'s `group by tweet_id` (SQLite's documented single-min/max form) AND by an earliest-capture dedupe inside the pure fn. `replied` = posted `reply_drafts.sourceTweetId` ‚ą© seen ids. 30d window (retention is 60d), `mode='timeline'` filter, no row limit (bounded by HV.1's 2,000/day cap). The denominator only exists because HV.2 captures **every** band including `skip`. Panel: a "Timeline funnel" section in `Playbook.tsx` after Model effectiveness, gated `insufficient data (n=‚Ä¶)` per cell.
> This file exists so `/plan-feature` never re-scans the repo. It is the single
> pre-computed answer to "where does X live and how is it wired".
> **Maintenance rule:** any commit that adds/moves/deletes a file, route, table,
> worker, extension surface, or pattern MUST update the touched section here (and
> re-stamp the header). Every plan produced by `/plan-feature` ends with a
> docs-sync task that includes this file.

## 1. Thirty-second orientation

Single-user service (one human, one bearer token) with four goals and a **hard
scope ceiling** (a feature not serving one of these does not get built):

1. Schedule X posts a week ahead (calendar + 60s publisher worker).
2. Track metrics over time on every published post (daily 03:00 UTC once-only snapshot pass).
3. Voice library ‚ÄĒ stash other people's tweets via $0 DOM scrape for style analysis.
4. Circles ‚ÄĒ the people layer: CRM stages, conversations/open loops, relationship-aware drafting, Playbook, warmth (quests/digest/icebreakers).

Runtime: **Bun ‚Č•1.1 + Hono** server on Hetzner (`https://stratus-narcis.duckdns.org`, systemd `stratus.service`, deployed via `scripts/deploy.sh`) + **Chrome MV3 side-panel extension** (Vite + React, loaded unpacked). State: **local SQLite via `bun:sqlite`** + Drizzle (`sqlite-core`), auto-migrated at boot. AI: xAI Grok via `src/grok/` (text `askGrok`, images `generateImages`). No queue, no Redis ‚ÄĒ in-process `setInterval` workers.

## 2. Root directory

| Path | What it is |
|---|---|

| `docs/PHASE-HISTORY.md` | Full chronological phase ledger (moved verbatim out of CLAUDE.md 2026-07-23). **Docs-sync tasks append their phase entry here, not in CLAUDE.md.** |
| `PLAN.md` | **Canonical build plan, goals 1‚Äď3** (cadence ladders, phased build). |
| `CIRCLES-PLAN.md` | **Canonical build plan, goal 4** (phases C0‚ÄďC10, all shipped; C10 = the notifications surface, planned separately in `plans/2026-07-16-notifications.md` and folded in at NT.7). |
| `SURFACES-PLAN.md` | Canonical plan for the S-phases (S0.x patches, S1 explorer, S2 MCP, S3 studio, S4 images). |
| `X-API-IMPLEMENTATION-PLAN.md` | Reference-only X API spec: endpoint semantics, pricing, policy quirks. Never a build plan. |
| `X-API-PRICING-REFERENCE.md` | Raw pricing tables. |
| `REPLY GUIDE.md` | The growth doctrine (70/30 ratio, reply bands, target roster) that features measure against. |
| `post prompt.md` / `reply prompt.md` / `thread prompt.md` | Prompt sources embedded verbatim as `POST_PROMPT_TEMPLATE` / `REPLY_PROMPT_TEMPLATE` / `THREAD_PROMPT_TEMPLATE` ‚ÄĒ **byte-sync asserted by bun:test**; edit .md and the TS literal together. **N.3:** post ¬ß1/¬ß5 bodies are now `{{PERSONA}}`/`{{BELIEFS}}` placeholders substituted from the active niche (in place, not tail ‚ÄĒ constant per niche). ¬ß6 palette + ¬ß9 hook examples still carry builder texture (D28 planning-error residual). **N.4:** reply "Who I am" body ‚Üí `{{REPLY_PERSONA}}` (heading + parenthetical stay). **AI.7:** `thread prompt.md` (new) = post ¬ß0‚Äď¬ß5 copied verbatim (same `{{PERSONA}}`/`{{BELIEFS}}`/`{{PILLARS}}`) + thread-specific job/output; tail placeholders `{{PILLARS}}`/`{{FEW_SHOT}}`/`{{IDEA}}`; literal in `src/x/posts/threadPrompt.ts`. |
| `OVERHAUL-PLAN.md`, `REPLY-MASTER-PLAN.md`, `RADAR-REVIEW.md`, `PEOPLE-GRAPH-PLAN.md`, `RELATIONSHIP-OS-PROPOSAL.md`, `MIGRATION-PLAN.md` | Historical/superseded planning docs ‚ÄĒ background only. |
| `MIGRATION-RUNBOOK.md` | Neon‚ÜíSQLite one-shot recovery runbook (runtime never touches Postgres). |
| `IPSE-Implementation-PRD.md` | The eventual big product. **Out of scope ‚ÄĒ never pull patterns from it.** |
| `MANUAL.md`, `DEPLOY.html`, `README.md` | User manual, deploy notes, readme. |
| `docs/` | Per-surface UI docs: one .md per extension tab + `s1`‚Äď`s4` + `s6` + `notifications-surface.md` (s5=Studio 2.0 is folded into `s3-studio.md`; `s6-augmented-ui.md` = the AX on-page chips/panel; `notifications-surface.md` = **NT.7** the C10 x.com/notifications augment + engagement harvest ‚ÄĒ both linked from README's "On x.com itself" table). Update the matching file when a tab changes. |
| `evals/` | Reply-quality eval scripts (`analyze-own-replies.ts` ‚ÄĒ the BAND crosstab) + CSV/md corpora. |
| `scripts/` | Deploy + one-shots + `smoke-*.ts` rerunnable checks (see ¬ß9). |
| `public/explorer.html` | S1 data-explorer UI shell (self-contained vanilla JS, served at `GET /explorer`, no build step). |
| `scrape.js`, `humantype.py`, `hammerspoon-init.lua` | Standalone helpers (console harvester origin; typing/paste automation). Not part of the server. |
| `engagement post prompt.md`, `engagement-calendar-14d.md`, `src/my_niche.md` | Content-strategy notes consumed by prompts/planning, not code. |
| `drizzle.config.ts` | Points drizzle-kit at `src/x/db/schema.ts` + `src/db/shared-schema.ts` ‚Üí `src/db/migrations/`. |
| `biome.json`, `tsconfig.json` | Lint/format; TS strict, `noEmit`, `allowImportingTsExtensions`; tsconfig `include` covers `scripts/**` + `drizzle.config.ts`. **biome `files.ignore` skips `dist`, `node_modules`, `scrape.js`, `Stratus Design System` (UI.8 ‚ÄĒ the DS folder is reference-only, not built), and `src/db/migrations` (UI.1 ‚ÄĒ drizzle-generated SQL + snapshot JSON; never hand-linted).** |
| `Stratus Design System/` | Reference-only design-system spec (Decision 9 ‚ÄĒ never imported/shipped). `tokens/{colors,typography,spacing,radii}.css` are the **source of the `--strat-*` tokens** UI.8 lifted into `styles.css`; `.jsx` components are specs the extension re-implements in TS. biome-ignored. |
| `.env.example` | Every env key, documented. Notables: `API_TOKEN` (one bearer for API+extension+MCP), `SELF_X_USER_ID`, `XAI_API_KEY`, `OPENROUTER_API_KEY` (AI.1 ‚ÄĒ second LLM provider; env-only, never in `app_settings`), `OPENROUTER_DAILY_BUDGET_USD` (AI.1 ‚ÄĒ soft, default 1.00, 0 disables), `SQLITE_PATH` (`:memory:` in tests), `X_DAILY_BUDGET_USD` (soft), `XAI_IMAGE_DAILY_BUDGET_USD` (hard 429), `DAILY_METRICS_ENABLED`, `WINNER_REREAD_MIN_VIEWS`, `STRATUS_DEPLOY_HOST`, `MENTION_API_REPLIES` (unread; verify-then-enable carve-out). |
| `.claude/` | `commands/ship.md`; skills: `stratus` (drive the HTTP API), `skill-explainer`, `plan-feature` (this skill), `masterplan` (executes `plans/MASTERPLAN.md` one task/session; state in its `STATE.md`; updates THIS codemap after every task). |
| `plans/` | 12 feature plans + `MASTERPLAN.md` (unified execution order, reasoning levels, waves, adaptations D1‚ÄďD10). Execution state: `.claude/skills/masterplan/STATE.md`. |

## 3. Server ‚ÄĒ `src/`

### 3.1 Entry + shared (platform-agnostic) layer

| File | Purpose |
|---|---|
| `src/app.ts` | Hono app. Order: CORS ‚Üí public `/healthz` ‚Üí `bearerAuth()` on `/x/*`, `/cost/*`, `/grok/*`, `/llm/*`, `/mcp` ‚Üí `cost` routes ‚Üí `mountX(app)` ‚Üí `mountGrok(app)` ‚Üí `mountLlm(app)` (always mounts ‚ÄĒ unlike mountGrok) ‚Üí `mountMcp(app)` (after mountX so curated tools find routes). `import.meta.main` gates `Bun.serve` + `startXWorkers()` + SIGTERM/SIGINT drain (30s force-exit). Importing from tests never binds a port. |
| `src/middleware/auth.ts` | Bearer guard (`API_TOKEN`). |
| `src/middleware/cors.ts` | `chrome-extension://*` always allowed + `ALLOWED_ORIGINS`. |
| `src/middleware/costTracker.ts` | `makeOnCost(platform, {dailyBudgetUsd})` ‚Üí writes `cost_events`, platform-tagged; soft budget watchdog logs `BUDGET WATCHDOG`. Platform-agnostic ‚ÄĒ never hardcode X here. |
| `src/db/client.ts` | The one `bun:sqlite` Database (WAL, `foreign_keys=ON`, boot auto-migrate). **Synchronous driver** ‚ÄĒ see ¬ß7 constraints. |
| `src/db/shared-schema.ts` | `cost_events` (platform free-text: `'x' \| 'grok' \| 'xai' \| 'openrouter'`; AI.1 added the union comment) + `app_settings` (UI.1 ‚ÄĒ `key`/JSON `value`/`updatedAt` override rows; a missing row = the registry default). |
| `src/settings/store.ts` | UI.1 **platform-agnostic** settings store: sync read-through over `app_settings` (module-level `Map` cache + invalidate-on-write), `getSetting`/`resolveSetting`/`getAllValues(scope?)`/`setSettings`(validate-all ‚Üí one-txn upsert)/`resetSettings`. Takes a `SettingsRegistry` (never imports `src/x/*`, like `costTracker` takes `platform`). |
| `src/db/migrations/` | `0000`‚Äď`0014` + meta (`0013` = `app_settings`, UI.1; `0014` = RU.2 reply `source` + radar `variants`/`model`/`reply_draft_id`). `0000` carries the `content_pillars` seed `INSERT OR IGNORE` ‚ÄĒ drizzle-kit generate drops seed INSERTs; re-check after every generate. biome-ignored (UI.1). |
| `src/routes/cost.ts` | `GET /cost/today` (per-platform spend + budget flags), `GET /cost/daily?days=` (zero-filled UTC series). |
| `src/routes/healthz.ts` | Public. 503 with `staleWorkers` when a heartbeat goes stale; reports `gitSha` from `.git-sha`; DB errors masked as `db_unreachable`. |
| `src/heartbeats.ts` | Worker heartbeat registry (`beat()` per tick; publisher stale >5min, dailyMetrics >25h). |
| `src/shared/replyBand.ts` | Canonical band classifier (hot/warm/skip/null) + `textLooksLikeReplyBait` ‚ÄĒ shared server/extension (extension re-export shim). |
| `src/shared/channelSuggest.ts` | Keyword‚Üíchannel suggestion (word-boundary matching), shared server/extension. |
| `src/mcp.ts` | S2 platform-agnostic MCP bridge: per-request stateless `McpServer` + `WebStandardStreamableHTTPServerTransport` at `POST /mcp`; calls `registerXTools`. |
| `src/test.test.ts` | Grab-bag pure-function suite (best-times, annotateGaps, pinnedSince/buildPinnedWatch, md_to_schedule ladders‚Ä¶). New tests should go in per-area files instead. |
| `src/app.test.ts` | Pre-DB route guards: bearer 401s, CORS preflight, calendar/thread/drafter validation. |

### 3.2 LLM providers ‚ÄĒ `src/grok/` (text+images) + `src/openrouter/` (AI.1) + `src/llm/` dispatcher (AI.2)

| File | Purpose |
|---|---|
| `grok/client.ts` | `askGrok` ‚ÄĒ ALL xAI text calls. `/v1/responses`, structured outputs via `text.format` json_schema (NOT `response_format`), `prompt_cache_key`, retry/auth, token pricing ‚Üí `cost_events` platform `'grok'`; warns on unknown model. |
| `grok/images.ts` | `generateImages` ‚ÄĒ ALL xAI image calls. `grok-imagine-image` default ($0.02/img; `-quality` $0.05 opt-in), `response_format:b64_json` (never let a raw xAI URL reach the extension ‚ÄĒ canvas taint), prefers response `usage.cost_in_usd_ticks` over the price table; platform `'xai'`. |
| `grok/pricing.ts` | Token + per-image price maps (`priceForImage`). |
| `grok/routes/ask.ts` | `POST /grok/ask` passthrough. |
| `grok/index.ts` | `mountGrok` (refuses to mount without `XAI_API_KEY`). |
| `openrouter/client.ts` | **AI.1** ‚ÄĒ `askOpenRouter`, the ONE place all OpenRouter calls go (a second LLM provider, sibling to grok). `POST /api/v1/chat/completions` (OpenAI shape), structured outputs via `response_format.json_schema` (NOT xAI's `text.format`), `usage:{include:true}` + `provider:{require_parameters:true}` ALWAYS; **cost comes straight off `usage.cost` (USD) ‚ÄĒ NO price table** (warns on a 2xx with tokens but no cost, ¬ß9.1); retry/auth/logCost mirror askGrok; `cost_events` platform `'openrouter'`; soft `OPENROUTER_DAILY_BUDGET_USD` watchdog (default $1.00, log-only). `DEFAULT_MODEL='anthropic/claude-sonnet-4.5'` (AI.2 settings own the real default); optional `fetchImpl` test seam; NO `promptCacheKey` (no OpenAI-compat field). INERT until AI.2 wires `askLLM`/`/llm` routes. |
| `openrouter/index.ts` | Re-exports only (`askOpenRouter`, `OpenRouterApiError`, `DEFAULT_MODEL`, types). No route/mount here ‚ÄĒ `/llm/*` lives in `src/llm/` (AI.2). |
| `llm/ask.ts` | **AI.2** ‚ÄĒ `askLLM(opts, {defaults})`, the provider dispatcher (¬ß7.1 extended: the ONE place picking grok vs openrouter; each provider keeps its own single entry point). Resolution `opts.provider ?? settings.provider`; merge precedence **opts > DB AI settings > call-site defaults** encoded once here (temperature/maxOutputTokens/reasoningEffort; model: openrouter‚Üí`opts.model ?? settings.openrouterModel`, grok‚Üí`opts.model` else askGrok's `grok-4.3`). A resolved provider whose env key is missing throws `LlmNotConfiguredError` ‚ÄĒ **never a silent fallback**. Forwards `fetchImpl` only on the openrouter path, `promptCacheKey` only on grok. Also `llmConfigured()` (either key set ‚ÄĒ the AI-layer runtime gate) / `llmProviderReady(p)` / pure `resolveProvider` / **`llmErrorPayload(err)`** (AI.5 ‚ÄĒ shared HTTP mapping: `LlmNotConfiguredError`‚Üí503 `llm_not_configured`, `GrokApiError`/`OpenRouterApiError`‚Üí429/502 `grok_upstream_error`/`openrouter_upstream_error`, else null so routes keep their generic branch). **LIVE (AI.5 + AI.6)** ‚ÄĒ call sites: replies single+batch, drafter, pillars/draft, voiceExtract, playbook extract-winners, digest, icebreaker. |
| `llm/settings.ts` | **AI.2** ‚ÄĒ `getAiSettings`/`saveAiSettings`/`parseAiPatch` over `app_settings` key `'ai'` (REUSES UI.1's table, D1; NOT a registry key so the UI.1 store never touches it). Read-through, NO cache (loadDoctrine discipline). `AiSettings{provider,openrouterModel,temperature|null,maxOutputTokens|null,reasoningEffort|null}`, defaults `grok`/`anthropic/claude-sonnet-4.5`/nulls. Field-by-field `sanitize` (garbage/schema-drift row ‚Üí defaults). **NO API keys here** ‚ÄĒ explorer/MCP-visible table (¬ß7.16, Decision 5); keys stay in env. |
| `llm/routes.ts` | **AI.2** ‚ÄĒ `GET/PATCH /llm/settings` (+ `providers:{grok,openrouter}` env flags; PATCH 400 per field, 409 `provider_not_configured` picking openrouter without its key, returns full settings), `GET /llm/models` (OpenRouter's free list, in-memory 1h cache, 503 `openrouter_not_configured` keyless). |
| `llm/index.ts` | `mountLlm(app)` (**always mounts**, unlike mountGrok) + re-exports `askLLM`/`llmConfigured`/`llmProviderReady`/`LlmNotConfiguredError` + settings helpers/types. |

### 3.3 X slice ‚ÄĒ `src/x/` (public surface = `index.ts` ONLY; nothing outside imports deeper)

**Primitives**

| File | Purpose |
|---|---|
| `index.ts` | `mountX(app)` + `startXWorkers()` + re-export `registerXTools`. **Read this first for any wiring change ‚ÄĒ mount order is load-bearing** (see ¬ß7 traps). LLM-gated mounts (**AI.6**): `replies`, `drafter`, `voiceExtract` only when `llmConfigured()` (EITHER `XAI_API_KEY` or `OPENROUTER_API_KEY`); `digest`/`playbook`/`pillars` mount always and check `llmConfigured()` at runtime (503); `images` stays `XAI_API_KEY`-only (Decision 6). |
| `client.ts` | `xFetch` ‚ÄĒ the ONE place all X API calls go (retries, RFC7807 parsing, rate-limit headers, `onCost`, `costHint`). Invariant #4. |
| `auth.ts` / `server.ts` / `token-store.ts` | OAuth2 PKCE; `bun run auth` callback server; single-row token store ‚ÄĒ refresh-token rotation persisted BEFORE return, serialized by in-process promise-chain mutex (invariant #3 ‚ÄĒ never reorder). |
| `endpoints.ts` | Typed wrappers: `getMe`, `getTweet`, `getTweetsByIds`, `searchRecent`, `getUserTweets`, `getUserMentions`, `createPost` (URL-surcharge + self-reply + self-quote gates), `deletePost`. Add one endpoint at a time, clamp `max_results` (invariant #5). |
| `fields.ts` / `errors.ts` / `pagination.ts` | Field defaults (`attachments` already included ‚ÄĒ rides free), `XApiError`+classify, `paginate` async iterator (`perPageSleepMs` for search/all). |
| `pricing.ts` | X price table keyed off endpoint substrings; call sites pass `costHint` when the path can't tell. |
| `db/schema.ts` | All 34 X tables (¬ß4). Type-imports `NicheDoctrine` from `niche/defaults.ts` (type-only, no runtime cycle). |
| `settings/registry.ts` | UI.1 typed settings catalog: `SettingDef`, `SETTINGS_REGISTRY` (doctrine group seeded), `validateSettingValue` (number/bool/string/enum/numberArray + sorted-unique), `settingsByGroup`. Implements the store's `SettingsRegistry` adapter + exports the **bound** `getSetting`/`resolveSetting`/`getAllValues`/`setSettings`/`resetSettings` ‚ÄĒ consumers import these, never the store. |
| `playground.ts` | `bun run play` scratch calls. |

**Domain modules (pure logic, bun-tested)**

| File | Purpose |
|---|---|
| `conversations.ts` | C2 thread grouping/ranking (`buildThreads`/`rankThreads`/`isActionable`) ‚ÄĒ no conversation table, regrouped per read. |
| `mentions.ts` | `pullMentions` ‚ÄĒ since_id checkpoint = max stored tweet_id; answered backfill; C1 person hooks. |
| `playbook.ts` | C4/S0.x aggregations, all gated `DEFAULT_MIN_CELL_N` (n‚Č•20): angles, pillar√óregister, structures, batch-vs-single (**RU.9:** `classifyReplyOrigin` takes a `postedTweetId‚Üíreply_drafts.source` map ‚ÄĒ a draft-linked reply is `radar` iff `source='radar'`, else `single`; the radar text-match heuristic is now only the fallback for replies with NO draft link, i.e. pre-tooling history; **RL.7:** a 4th param `cannedTexts: ReadonlySet<string>` of normalized `reply_list_uses.renderedText` is checked LAST ‚ÄĒ a canned use leaves no `reply_drafts` row, so rendered text is its only evidence; `ReplyOrigin` = `'single'|'radar'|'canned'`, `BatchVsSingle` gains a `canned` cell, and a reply that is both a posted draft and a text match counts once, as the draft), band calibration, relationship lift, media (S0.2), latency (S0.5), roster coverage (S0.7), idea payoff (S0.8), **personal-context lift (`buildMeEffectiveness`, ME.5 ‚ÄĒ replies split by `contextSnapshot.me` present/absent; `withMe`/`withoutMe`/`totalMeasured`, clone of relationship lift + a `totalMeasured` field for the partition invariant)**, **model effectiveness (`buildModelEffectiveness`, AI.12 ‚ÄĒ posted replies bucketed by raw `reply_drafts.model` string [`/` = provider, never parsed]; `{cells: ModelCell[], totalMeasured}`, cells most-sampled-first, each independently gated; **no lift line** ‚ÄĒ buckets only, no baseline pair; the OpenRouter-experiment judge)**, **timeline opportunity funnel (`buildTimelineFunnel`, HV.5 ‚ÄĒ ¬ß12, NOT ¬ß11 which AI.12 took; `TimelineSeenRow{tweetId,views,comments,text,tweetTimeMs|null,capturedAtMs}` + `deriveTimelineBand` [ageMin = capturedAt‚ąítweetTime, vpm = views/max(ageMin,1), bait = `textLooksLikeReplyBait`, fed to shared `classifyBand`] ‚Üí `{cells: FunnelCell[], totalSeen, totalReplied}`; `TimelineBand = Band | 'unknown'` where **`'unknown'` = no tweet time (no age ‚áí no velocity ‚áí nothing to classify) and NEVER folds into the real `null` band**; rows are deduped to their **first sighting** (earliest `capturedAtMs`) inside the pure fn too, so a re-scrolled viral thread can't re-band itself; per-cell gate on `seen`, `rate = replied/seen` null under it)**. |
| `quests.ts` | C9 daily quests (vacuous-done contract ‚ÄĒ a quiet day never breaks the streak). |
| `digest.ts` | C9 Sunday digest facts assembly (pure; one LLM narration in the route, cached in `digests`). **ME.5:** `DigestGoal` + `DigestFacts.goals` (active `me_goals` + progress; null when none, passthrough in `buildDigestFacts`). **AI.6:** `DIGEST_INSTRUCTIONS` ‚Üí exported `DIGEST_PROMPT_TEMPLATE` (registry default, key `digest`, `{{FACTS}}` at the tail); `buildDigestInput(facts, template = DIGEST_PROMPT_TEMPLATE)` substitutes via local split/join (no registry import ‚ÄĒ cycle) ‚ÄĒ byte-identical to the old concatenation. |
| `conversion.ts` | S0.1 profile-visit ‚Üí follow conversion math. |
| `people/stage.ts` | Stage engine: stranger‚Üínoticed‚Üíengaged‚Üíresponded‚Üímutual (‚Č•2 exchange days)‚Üíally (‚Č•4/60d); ratchets up only. **NT.2:** `PERSON_EVENT_TYPES` gained `their_like`/`their_repost`/`their_follow` and they are in **no** stage set (not NOTICED/INBOUND/OUTBOUND) ‚ÄĒ engagement is not reciprocity, so 50 likes + a follow is still `stranger` (C10 decision 1, matrix-tested; do not re-litigate). |
| `people/store.ts` | All people writes: `upsertPerson` (fill-only default, overwrite for profile scrapes), `logPersonEvents`/`safeLogPersonEvents` (deterministic ids `type:ref_table:ref_id` + INSERT OR IGNORE), `loadRelationshipFacts(Safe)`. |
| `people/relationship.ts` | C3 relationship block render (server-stamped, variable-tail). |
| `people/angles.ts` | Per-person angle crosstab. |
| `people/followups.ts` | C5 classifier: chain_live > dm_ready > neglected_target > neglected_ally > momentum; S0.6 `pickReupCandidate`; snooze keys `kind:handle` / `reup:<tweetId>`. |
| `people/sightings.ts` | C6 hover-capture ingest (once/day/handle event + snapshot gates). |
| `people/engagements.ts` | **NT.2** ‚ÄĒ C10 notification-harvest ingest (sightings.ts mirror). `MAX_ENGAGEMENTS_PER_BATCH=50`, `EngagementKind` = like\|repost\|follow (the parser's `'other'` is dropped client-side and is deliberately not representable), `dedupeEngagements` (key `kind:handle:targetText`, freshest wins), `engagementEventId` (`their_like:notif:<handle>:<tweetId>` ‚Üí day-bucket `‚Ä¶:<YYYY-MM-DD>` when unresolved ‚Üí `their_follow:notif:<handle>` once ever), pure `matchTargetTweetId(snippet, posts)` (collapsed-whitespace **prefix** match, ‚Č•20 chars or null) + DB wrapper `resolveTargetTweetId`, `recordEngagements` ‚Üí `{received, processed, skipped, events}` (fill-only upsert `source:'notification'`, INSERT OR IGNORE events with `refTable/refId: null`, own-post window loaded **once per batch** and not at all for a follow-only batch, `recomputePerson` once per distinct handle = watermarks only). **NT.3:** `ENGAGEMENT_KINDS` + the `isEngagementKind` guard live here beside the union (`isStage`/`isFollowupKind` idiom) ‚ÄĒ `POST /x/people/engagements` is their only caller and the enforcement point for the parser's `'other'`. |
| `people/icebreakers.ts` | C9 grounding renderer (refusal ladder BEFORE key check: 404 ‚Üí 422 no_shared_context). **AI.6:** `ICEBREAKER_INSTRUCTIONS` ‚Üí exported `ICEBREAKER_PROMPT_TEMPLATE` (registry default, key `icebreaker`, `{{GROUNDING}}` at the tail); `buildIcebreakerInput(grounding, template = ICEBREAKER_PROMPT_TEMPLATE)` substitutes via local split/join ‚ÄĒ byte-identical to the old concatenation. |
| `niche/defaults.ts` | **N0.1** ‚ÄĒ lowest niche layer (imports nothing from prompt/route/store, pillars.ts pattern). `NicheDoctrine` (5 knobs), `DEFAULT_DOCTRINE` (10/20/70/2/10), `Niche` type, `DEFAULT_NICHE` (`builder`; persona/beliefs/replyPersona lifted **verbatim** from post ¬ß1/¬ß5 + reply "Who I am", description from `src/my_niche.md` ‚ÄĒ post ¬ß1/¬ß5 moved at N.3, reply "Who I am" moved at N.4; all guarded byte-exact by the equivalence fixtures in `src/test.test.ts`), `NICHE_SLUG_RE` (=PILLAR_SLUG_RE), `resolveDoctrine` (lenient field-by-field: finite positive wins, else default). |
| `niche/store.ts` | **N0.1** ‚ÄĒ only reader of `niches`: `loadActiveNiche()` (active row else `DEFAULT_NICHE` when none), `loadActiveNicheSafe()` (never throws ‚Üí default, ¬ß7.8), `loadDoctrine()` (resolveDoctrine of the safe active niche). **Post-side consumers wired at N.3** (drafter + pillars/draft), **reply side at N.4** (replies single + batch); **doctrine wired at N.5** ‚ÄĒ `loadDoctrine()` feeds `targetBand` multipliers + brief reply quota/ratio (voice, brief, followups, playbook, digest). |
| `me/profile.ts` | **ME.1** ‚ÄĒ pure Me/profile layer (relationship.ts pattern: no DB, callers pass `now`). `ME_KINDS`/`GOAL_KINDS`, window consts (`EMOTION_WINDOW_DAYS=7`/`EVENT_WINDOW_DAYS=30`, inclusive boundary; facts/notes evergreen; `pinned` overrides window+cap), per-kind caps + render hard-caps (`MAX_POST_LINES=14`/`MAX_POST_CHARS=1200`, brief `‚Č§3`/`300`), `ME_INSTRUCTION`/`ME_BRIEF_INSTRUCTION` (instruction rides INSIDE the block, ¬ß7.18), `selectEntriesForPrompt`, `goalProgress`/`resolveGoals` (followers ‚Üź account_snapshots value, mrr/custom ‚Üź manual currentValue; null when no data), `renderMeContext`/`renderMeBrief` (`''` when empty ‚Üí no injection ‚Üí prompts byte-identical). Loader `loadMeContextSafe` wired at **ME.2** (`routes/me.ts`); **ME.3** injects the rendered block at all three draft-prompt tails (post drafter + reply single + reply batch). |
| `niche/wizard.ts` | **N0.8** ‚ÄĒ pure wizard module (pillarDraft.ts pattern): `NICHE_WIZARD_SCHEMA` (structured-outputs `{slug,label,description,persona,beliefs,replyPersona,pillars[3],channels[‚Č§5 w/ keywords]}`), `buildNicheWizardInput(description)` (instruction+anatomy prefix, DEFAULT_NICHE+DEFAULT_PILLARS as the in-prompt EXAMPLE, user description at the variable TAIL ¬ß7.15), `parseNicheProposal(raw)` (lenient: coerces slugs to kebab-case, enforces exactly-3 distinct pillars + required non-empty text + length ceilings 120/10000 mirroring the CRUD routes; a malformed channel is dropped not fatal; junk/bad-slug/wrong-count ‚Üí null). Consumed only by `POST /x/niche/draft`. |
| `posts/prompt.ts` | `POST_PROMPT_TEMPLATE` (byte-synced with `post prompt.md`) + drafter helpers, `buildPostDraftsSchema(slugs)`. **N.3:** `PERSONA_PLACEHOLDER`/`BELIEFS_PLACEHOLDER`; `BuildPostDraftOptions.persona?/beliefs?` (default `DEFAULT_NICHE`) substituted FIRST, in place. **ME.3:** `BuildPostDraftOptions.meContext?` appended at the variable tail before `guidance` (empty ‚Üí no change). **AI.3:** `BuildPostDraftOptions.template?` ‚ÄĒ the registry-loaded body (default `POST_PROMPT_TEMPLATE`, so callers/tests untouched). |
| `posts/pillars.ts` | `DEFAULT_PILLARS`, `parsePillar`. |
| `posts/threadPrompt.ts` | **AI.7** ‚ÄĒ thread drafter (pure): `THREAD_PROMPT_TEMPLATE` (byte-synced with `thread prompt.md`; post ¬ß0‚Äď¬ß5 verbatim + thread job/output), `buildThreadDraftSchema(slugs)` (`{pillar enum, tweets string[]}` ‚ÄĒ **no minItems/maxItems**, N.8/RU.3 rejection-risk convention; count steered by prompt), `parseThreadDraft(raw, slugs) ‚Üí {pillar, tweets, overLong}|null` (‚Č•2 tweets, bad pillar ‚Üí null, 280-over `overLong` positions computed not rejected), `buildThreadDraftInput(opts)` (persona/beliefs in place; pillar+tweetCount+idea folded into the single `{{FEW_SHOT}}`/`{{IDEA}}` tail ‚ÄĒ no `{{PILLAR}}` token; meContext+guidance appended). Imports only types/consts from `posts/prompt.ts` (no cycle). |
| `posts/rewritePrompt.ts` | **AI.8** ‚ÄĒ rewrite assist (pure, **TS-only ‚ÄĒ Decision 9, no `.md`/byte-sync**): `REWRITE_PROMPT_TEMPLATE` (`{{DRAFT}}`/`{{INSTRUCTION}}` at the tail; **no persona/pillar token** ‚Üí cache bucket unaffected by niche), `REWRITE_SCHEMA` (static `{variants:[{text, kind}]}`, kind enum `tightened|rehooked|restructured`, **no minItems/maxItems**), `MAX_VARIANT_LENGTH=560`, `parseRewrite(raw, maxLen=560) ‚Üí RewriteVariant[]|null` (null on malformed `variants`; empty/over-long/unknown-kind entries dropped ‚ÄĒ array may be `[]`), `buildRewriteInput({draft, instruction?, template?})` (split/join $-safe; missing instruction ‚Üí `(none ‚ÄĒ just sharpen it)`). No DB, no niche import. |
| `posts/ideasPrompt.ts` | **AI.9** ‚ÄĒ idea generator (pure, **TS-only ‚ÄĒ Decision 9, no `.md`/byte-sync**): `IDEAS_PROMPT_TEMPLATE` (`{{PILLARS}}`/`{{WINNERS}}`/`{{STEER}}` at the tail; **no persona/belief token** ‚Üí cache bucket niche-independent even though the rendered pillars are niche-scoped, since pillars sit at the variable tail), `IDEAS_SCHEMA` (static `{ideas:[{text,pillar,angle}]}`, angle enum `observation|stance|story|question`, **`pillar` a FREE string not enum-bound** so a mis-tag is nulled not dropped; **no minItems/maxItems**), `MAX_IDEA_TEXT=500`/`MAX_IDEA_COUNT=10`, `parseIdeaProposals(raw, allowedSlugs, maxCount=10) ‚Üí IdeaProposal[]|null` (null on malformed `ideas`; empty/over-long/unknown-angle entries dropped; a pillar outside `allowedSlugs` ‚Üí **null, not dropped**; clamped to maxCount ‚ÄĒ array may be `[]`), `buildIdeasInput({pillars?, winners, steer?, count?, template?})` (split/join $-safe; count folds into the {{STEER}} block like threadPrompt folds tweetCount; empty winners/steer ‚Üí placeholder text). No DB, no niche import. |
| `posts/pillarDraft.ts` | AI pillar proposal (never persisted directly). **N.3:** hardcoded compact `PERSONA` deleted ‚ÄĒ `BuildPillarDraftOptions.persona?` (default `DEFAULT_NICHE.persona`); the route passes niche.persona+description. **AI.5:** the persona+format block is now `PILLAR_DRAFT_TEMPLATE` (registry default, key `pillar-draft`) with `{{PERSONA}}` (optional, in-place first) + `{{EXISTING_PILLARS}}`/`{{JOB}}` (required); `BuildPillarDraftOptions.template?`; the job strings stay code-built. |
| `replies/prompt.ts` | `REPLY_PROMPT_TEMPLATE` (byte-synced with `reply prompt.md`; **RU.1**: 3 variants, one per angle extends/contrarian/debate), `buildGrokInput`, `buildBatchGrokInput` (**AI.5**: renders the standalone `REPLY_BATCH_PROMPT_TEMPLATE` ‚ÄĒ the heading-slicing `sharedVoiceBlock`/`batchReplyHead`/`VOICE_BLOCK_END` machinery is GONE; the batch default embeds the reply default's voice block verbatim, locked by the anti-drift test in `src/test.test.ts`; `{{POSTS}}`/`{{IDEA}}` substitute at the tail with the token-missing fallbacks preserved for pre-token overrides; the C3 relationship note rides inside the POSTS value; **RU.3**: 3 variants/post, `BatchReply={tweetId,variants[]}`, `parseBatchReplies` validates ‚Č•1 variant/entry), `parseContext`/`parseBatchTweets` (NEVER accept `relationship`/`guidance`/`niche` from clients ‚ÄĒ whitelist builders), `BATCH_REPLY_SCHEMA` (`{replies:[{id,variants:[{text,angle}]}]}`). **N.4:** "Who I am" body ‚Üí `{{REPLY_PERSONA}}` (`REPLY_PERSONA_PLACEHOLDER`); `buildGrokInput`/`buildBatchGrokInput` gain trailing `opts?: {replyPersona?}` (default `DEFAULT_NICHE.replyPersona`), substituted FIRST/token-tolerant via `substituteReplyPersona` (batch: over the effective template before POSTS/IDEA land); `PostContext.niche?: {slug}` server-stamped. **ME.3:** `PostContext.me?` server-stamped (parseContext allowlist never accepts it) ‚ÄĒ `buildGrokInput` appends it at the tail after relationship (order relationship‚Üíme‚Üíguidance); `buildBatchGrokInput`'s opts bag gains `meBrief?`, appended ONCE per batch after guidance. **AI.3/AI.5:** BOTH builders' opts bags carry `template?` (registry body; per-request `override` still beats it). |
| `replyLists/engine.ts` | **RL.1** ‚ÄĒ canned-reply engine (pure, followups.ts style: no DB, no clock, no `Math.random` ‚ÄĒ callers inject `rng`). `MAX_REPLY_LENGTH=280`, `TEMPLATE_VARS` (`name`/`first_name`/`handle`), `DEFAULT_HUMANIZER` (prefix .25 / suffix .20 / lowercase .15 / drop-period .10 / typo .05 ‚ÄĒ opening guesses; per-list JSON overrides), `parseHumanizerConfig` (lenient field-by-field, **null ONLY on a non-object** ‚ÄĒ that's what lets RL.2's CRUD 400 an invalid humanizer) + `resolveHumanizer`, `renderTemplate` (a missing var takes ONE adjacent separator with it ‚Üí "Thank you!"; unknown `{foo}` verbatim; emoji/flags stripped from the name), `templateVars`/`availableVarsFor`, `pickItem` (anti-repeat: var-needing items deprioritized, `min(n-1, floor(n/2))` most-recent excluded, uniform pick among the rest ‚ÄĒ no repeat at n‚Č•2), `humanize` (**fixed `HUMANIZE_DRAWS`=10 draws whether or not a step fires**, so a stubbed sequence maps to steps by position; names/handles/`@`/`#`/links are protected spans never typo'd; an overflowing prefix/suffix is skipped, never truncated), `composeReply`. |
| `replyLists/generate.ts` | **RL.4** ‚ÄĒ reply-list AI item generator (pure, **TS-only ‚ÄĒ Decision 9, no `.md`/byte-sync**): `REPLY_LIST_PROMPT_TEMPLATE` (registry default, key `reply-list`; `{{COUNT}}`/`{{REQUEST}}`/`{{EXISTING_ITEMS}}` all required and all at the tail ‚ÄĒ **no persona token**, so the cacheable prefix is niche-independent and the route's cache key needs no `:slug:updatedAtMs` suffix, same as `ideas`/`rewrite`), `REPLY_LIST_GEN_SCHEMA` (`{items:[{text}]}`, no minItems/maxItems ‚ÄĒ the strict-mode rejection-risk convention), `buildListGenInput({prompt, count?, existingItems?, template?})` (split/join $-safe; empty list ‚Üí `(none yet ‚ÄĒ this list is empty)`; existing items capped at 30), `parseGeneratedItems(raw, maxCount=30) ‚Üí {text}[]|null` (**null only when `items` is missing/not an array**; empty + >`MAX_REPLY_LENGTH` entries dropped; **dedupe key is lowercased + whitespace-collapsed**, since casing-only twins defeat the anti-repeat pick; `[]` is a legal "nothing survived" the route 502s on). `DEFAULT_GENERATED_ITEMS`=12 / `MAX_GENERATED_ITEMS`=30 / `MAX_GEN_PROMPT_LEN`=2000. |
| `prompts/registry.ts` | **AI.3** ‚ÄĒ the editable-prompt catalog: `PROMPT_KEYS` (**RL.4: 11 keys ‚ÄĒ `reply`/`reply-batch`/`post`/`thread`/`rewrite`/`ideas`/`voice-extract`/`pillar-draft`/`digest`/`icebreaker`/`reply-list`** ‚ÄĒ new keys append at the end; defaults from pure modules, `ideas` from `posts/ideasPrompt.ts`, `reply-list` from `replyLists/generate.ts`), `isPromptKey`, `PROMPT_SPECS` (name/description/`defaultBody` = the byte-synced templates + `required`/`optional` placeholder sets; **defaults import from PURE modules only ‚ÄĒ a route-file import would cycle**), `loadPrompt(key)`/`loadPromptSafe` (¬ß7.8 ‚ÄĒ `prompt_overrides` row else default; row presence IS `customized`; sha-8 `cacheKey`, call sites append the niche `:slug:updatedAtMs` suffix), `validatePromptBody` (`{ok,missing,unknown}` ‚ÄĒ required must survive an edit, niche placeholders optional/token-tolerant, unknown `{{A_Z}}` deduped warning), `renderPrompt` (split/join, $-safe; for later-task call sites), `promptCacheKey`. Imports the prompt modules for defaults incl. `digest.ts`/`people/icebreakers.ts` (AI.6 ‚ÄĒ both pure-ish, no registry import; no cycle: routes ‚Üí registry ‚Üí templates). |
| `voice/extractPrompt.ts` | **AI.5** ‚ÄĒ pure ¬ß8.3 extraction pieces moved out of `routes/voiceExtract.ts` (registry-cycle avoidance): `EXTRACT_PROMPT_TEMPLATE` (registry default, key `voice-extract`, `{{TWEET_TEXT}}` at the tail ‚ÄĒ renders byte-identical to the old `EXTRACT_PROMPT_PREFIX + text`), `TEMPLATE_SCHEMA`, `TEMPLATE_LENGTHS`/`TemplateLength`/`ExtractedTemplate`, `parseExtractedTemplate`, `TEMPLATE_EXTRACT_MAX_OUTPUT_TOKENS`. Consumed by `routes/voiceExtract.ts` + `routes/playbook.ts`. |
| `data/inspect.ts` | S1 read-only core: second `{readonly:true}` connection (`:memory:` falls back to primary), whitelist from Drizzle exports (**`tokens` excluded entirely**), `readTable` (validated identifiers, escaped LIKE), `runSelect` (single-statement SELECT/WITH, 500-row cap), `describeTable`. Reused by MCP schema tools. |
| `mcp.ts` | S2 `registerXTools` ‚ÄĒ 19 tools: 3 schema (inspect core), 12 curated (in-process `app.request` with forwarded bearer; `x_digest` forces `factsOnly`; **N0.2 added `x_niche`** ‚Üí `GET /x/niche`; **M1.6 added `x_me`** ‚Üí `GET /x/me`), 4 write ($0 only; `x_draft_post` hard-codes `status:'draft'`; **M1.6 added `x_add_me_entry`** ‚Üí `POST /x/me/entries`, zod enum restricts `kind` to the 4 ME_KINDS ‚ÄĒ no goal write, journal only). |

**Workers ‚ÄĒ `src/x/workers/`**

| File | Purpose |
|---|---|
| `publisher.ts` | 60s tick. Claim txn (`pending‚Üípublishing` committed BEFORE `createPost`) ‚Üí finalize; 4xx‚Üí`failed`, 5xx/network ‚Üí stuck `publishing` (ambiguous, shouted every tick, reconcile resolves). Threads: self-replies ~500ms apart, one bad segment freezes the rest (`thread_frozen`); re-verifies self-quote ownership. |
| `dailyMetrics.ts` | 03:00 UTC: getMe ‚Üí `account_snapshots` (1/UTC-day, + `pinned_tweet_id`); since_id discovery of own tweets (stamps `has_media`); snapshot every non-retired row ‚ÄĒ **retire batch BEFORE writing snapshots** (invariant #7); winner re-read (‚Č§5/day, claim pollCount 1‚Üí2 before the billed call); `pullMentions`. |

### 3.4 HTTP routes ‚ÄĒ `src/x/routes/` (all under `/x`, bearer-guarded unless noted)

| Router file | Endpoints (method path ‚ÄĒ one-line semantics) |
|---|---|
| `brief.ts` | `GET /brief` ‚ÄĒ Today-tab payload: KPI+sparkline, yesterday, leaders, plan+annotated gaps (S0.4), reply quota, ratio, spend, quests+streak (C9), pinnedWatch (S0.9). `?tzOffsetMin=` local-day; spend stays UTC. Pure helpers `pinnedSince`/`buildPinnedWatch` live here. **N.5:** the old `REPLY_TARGET`/`WEEK_REPLY_TARGET_PCT` consts are gone ‚ÄĒ reply quota/ratio target + the target-roster band all read `loadDoctrine()` (one sync SELECT/request). |
| `calendar.ts` | `POST /posts/scheduled` (URL guard on pending; optional validated `pillar` ‚ÄĒ validates via `getActivePillars()`, so it **inherits the N.6 active-niche filter** for free, no code change), `POST /posts/threads`, `GET /posts/scheduled` (+filters), `GET/PATCH/DELETE /posts/scheduled/:id` (worker-owned statuses 409; PATCH `media_note`; GET returns thread siblings + `seededBy`). |
| `metrics.ts` | `GET /metrics/replies`, `/metrics/posts`, `/metrics/account` (**S5.5** the Studio milestone card's client `api.metrics.account()` consumes this ‚ÄĒ `{count,latest,series}`, `AccountSeriesPoint`), `/metrics/best-times` (`?tzOffsetMin=`, top gated n‚Č•3), `/metrics/pillars`, `/metrics/:tweetId`. |
| `posts.ts` | `POST /posts/reconcile` ‚ÄĒ triggers the daily pass manually. |
| `pillars.ts` | `GET/POST /pillars`, `PATCH/DELETE /pillars/:slug` (last-active 409), `POST /pillars/draft` (proposal, runtime `llmConfigured()` check ‚Üí 503 `grok_not_configured` AI.6; **N.3** grounds on active niche persona+description; **AI.5** `loadPromptSafe('pillar-draft')` ‚Üí `template` into `buildPillarDraftInput`, `askLLM` w/ defaults low/700/0.7, body `provider` accepted, cache key `` `${prompt.cacheKey}:${slug}:${updatedAtMs}` `` ‚ÄĒ `PILLAR_DRAFT_CACHE_KEY` gone). **N.6:** all reads scoped by `ownedByNiche(activeSlug)` = `niche = active.slug OR niche IS NULL` (legacy tolerance); POST stamps `niche = loadActiveNicheSafe().slug`; `getActivePillars()` falls back to `DEFAULT_PILLARS` **only when active niche is `builder`** (else `[]` ‚ÄĒ the drafter refusal trigger); last-active 409 guard counts **within the active niche's set** (DELETE only guards when the target belongs to that set, so it can't false-fire on another niche's pillar). |
| `prompts.ts` | **AI.4** ‚ÄĒ the prompt editor over `prompt_overrides` (always mounted next to `pillars` ‚ÄĒ works with no LLM key). `GET /prompts` (list: key/name/description/required/`customized`=row-presence/`updatedAt`), `GET /prompts/:key` (body+`defaultBody`+customized+required, for diff/reset), `PATCH /prompts/:key {body}` (‚Č§32KB ‚Üí 413 `body_too_large`; `validatePromptBody` ‚Üí 400 `missing_placeholder`+`missing`; upsert ‚Üí `{customized:true, unknownPlaceholders}`), `POST /prompts/:key/reset` (delete row ‚Üí `{customized:false}`), `POST /prompts/restore-defaults` (delete ALL ‚Üí `{restored:n}`); unknown key ‚Üí 404 `unknown_prompt`. Reuses the AI.3 registry; static `restore-defaults` + `:key/reset` param don't collide (¬ß7.20, different segment counts). |
| `niche.ts` | **N0.2** ‚ÄĒ `GET /niche` (active niche + resolved doctrine, `DEFAULT_NICHE` fallback), `GET /niches` (active-first), `POST /niches` (created INACTIVE, 409 `slug_exists`), `PATCH /niches/:slug` (edit + doctrine; `active:true` ‚Üí atomic swap in a **sync** txn; `active:false` on the only active ‚Üí 409 `last_active_niche`), `DELETE /niches/:slug` (409 `niche_active` if active; owned pillars/channels keep their stamp). Validation mirrors pillars; doctrine rejects non-positive/non-numeric (no silent coerce). Always mounted, $0. **N0.8:** `POST /niche/draft` (the wizard) ‚ÄĒ `{description ‚Č§5000}` ‚Üí one `askGrok` structured-outputs call (effort low, `maxOutputTokens` 2500, cache key `stratus-niche-wizard`) ‚Üí parsed `NicheProposal` (never persisted). Description validated (400 `invalid_description`) BEFORE the runtime XAI key check (503 `grok_not_configured`) so the $0 guards are testable without a key; the paid call is last (¬ß7.4). `POST /niche/draft` ‚Č† `POST /niches` ‚ÄĒ no `:slug` collision. |
| `me.ts` | **ME.2** ‚ÄĒ `GET /me?kind=&active=` (entries each w/ server-computed `inWindow` via `isEntryInWindow`; goals each w/ `progress`), `POST/PATCH/DELETE /me/entries[/:id]` (kind/text‚Č§1000/happenedAt-ISO/pinned/active; per-field 400 codes), `POST/PATCH/DELETE /me/goals[/:id]` (label/kind/target>0/unit/deadline/currentValue/status), `GET /me/context?mode=post\|reply` ‚Üí `{mode, block\|null}` (the exact injected block, ¬ß7.18). Exports **`loadMeContextSafe(mode)`** ‚ÄĒ active entries + active goals + latest `account_snapshots` followers ‚Üí `selectEntriesForPrompt`/`resolveGoals` ‚Üí render; null on empty OR any error (¬ß7.8, never throws). Always mounted, $0 (pure SQL). Static `/me` prefix + `:id` params shadow nothing (¬ß7.20). **ME.3** consumes `loadMeContextSafe` in `drafter.ts` (post) + `routes/replies.ts` (single stamps `ctx.me`, batch passes `meBrief`). |
| `drafter.ts` | `POST /posts/draft` (3 register-distinct drafts ‚Üí `status='draft'` rows), `POST /posts/reup` (self-quote drafts; ownership via posts_published), **`POST /posts/draft-thread`** (**AI.7** ‚ÄĒ `{idea?,ideaId?,pillar?,tweetCount?,model?,provider?,reasoningEffort?}` ‚Üí one structured-outputs call via `loadPromptSafe('thread')` + `buildThreadDraftInput`/`buildThreadDraftSchema` ‚Üí `insertThreadDraft` lands a `status='draft'` head + `status='segment'` tails sharing a threadId, `source='drafter'`; **one auto-regenerate** if a segment >280 chars (nudge names them, still-long ‚Üí 502 `thread_invalid`); `tweetCount` non-int ‚Üí 400 `invalid_tweet_count`, clamp 3‚Äď8; `consumeIdeaSafe` after insert; URL allowed in drafts. `insertThreadDraft(pillar,tweets,ideaId?)` exported for the route test), **`POST /posts/rewrite`** (**AI.8** ‚ÄĒ `{text [1‚Äď2000], instruction? [‚Č§500], model?, provider?}` ‚Üí inline validation [`invalid_body`/`invalid_text`/`invalid_instruction`/`invalid_model`/`invalid_provider`, all pre-spend] ‚Üí `loadPromptSafe('rewrite')` + `buildRewriteInput` ‚Üí `askLLM` [defaults 0.7/900/low, cache key = bare `prompt.cacheKey`] ‚Üí **no DB rows**; `parseRewrite` null ‚Üí 502 `rewrite_parse_error`, `[]` ‚Üí 502 `rewrite_invalid`; over-long variants dropped, never truncated). LLM-gated mount (**AI.6** `llmConfigured()`). **N.3:** `generateAndInsert` loads `loadActiveNicheSafe()`, passes persona/beliefs, cache key `` `${PROMPT_CACHE_KEY}:${slug}:${updatedAtMs}` ``. **N.6:** both routes refuse `409 {error:'no_pillars_for_niche', niche}` when `getActivePillars()` is `[]` (a custom niche with no active pillars) ‚ÄĒ BEFORE any Grok spend (¬ß7.4). `POST /pillars/draft` deliberately does NOT refuse (empty `existing` is how the first pillar is made). **AI.3:** the prompt comes from `loadPromptSafe('post')` (`template` into `buildPostDraftInput`), cache key `` `${prompt.cacheKey}:${slug}:${updatedAtMs}` `` (static `PROMPT_CACHE_KEY` gone). **AI.5:** `generateAndInsert` calls `askLLM` (defaults temp 0.7/600/low); `parseCommon` accepts `provider` (400 `invalid_provider`) and returns `reasoningEffort` only when body-supplied (house default rides the defaults tier); errors via `llmErrorPayload`. |
| `replies.ts` | `POST /replies/generate` (band gate 422 BEFORE spend ‚Üí relationship+guidance stamp ‚Üí 3 variants, `MAX_OUTPUT_TOKENS=520` ‚Üí specificity gate w/ one auto-regen), `POST /replies/generate-batch` (‚Č§25, **3 variants/post RU.3**, `maxOutputTokens=min(9000,200+n*420)`, response items `{tweetId,text,angle,variants}` primary=variants[0], no DB rows, persists `radar_drafts`), `GET /replies`, `/replies/outcomes` (¬ß6.2 join), `/replies/default-prompt`, `GET/PATCH/DELETE /replies/:id` (PATCH‚Üíposted = paste time, logs my_reply, backfills postedTweetId). LLM-gated mount (**AI.6** `llmConfigured()`). **N.4:** both generate paths `loadActiveNicheSafe()` (single: AFTER the band gate ‚ÄĒ refuse-before-work), pass `replyPersona`, stamp `ctx.niche={slug}` pre-insert (contextSnapshot per-niche key), cache keys niche-suffixed `:slug:updatedAtMs`. **AI.3:** single generate loads `loadPromptSafe('reply')` AFTER the band gate (`template` into the opts bag ‚ÄĒ a client `systemPromptOverride` still beats it), cache key `` `${prompt.cacheKey}:${slug}:${updatedAtMs}` ``; `GET /replies/default-prompt` returns the effective (override-aware) registry body. **AI.5:** both generate paths call `askLLM` (house defaults temp 0.7 / 520 & the computed batch cap / effort low via the defaults tier ‚ÄĒ a stored AI setting sits between body opts and them, D44), accept body `provider` (400 `invalid_provider`, validated before the band gate), and map errors via `llmErrorPayload`; batch loads `loadPromptSafe('reply-batch')` (standalone template, cache key niche-suffixed like single ‚ÄĒ `BATCH_PROMPT_CACHE_KEY` gone). **RU.8:** `parseBatchTweets` accepts `band:'manual'` (a ‚äē pinned tweet ‚ÄĒ queue metadata, still never reaches Grok). |
| `voice.ts` | `POST /voice/scrape`, `PUT /voice/authors/:handle` (enrich + snapshot append), `GET /voice/authors`, `PATCH/DELETE /voice/authors/:handle`, `GET /voice/targets` (target band + momentum), `GET /voice/tweets` (filters), `PATCH /voice/tweets/:tweetId` (`tags`/`addTags`), `DELETE /voice/tweets/:tweetId`. Exports `loadTargetHandles`. All $0. **N.5:** `targetBand(myFollowers, band={minX:2,maxX:10})` ‚ÄĒ the multipliers now come from `loadDoctrine()` (default keeps every call site/test green); call sites in voice/brief/followups/playbook/digest pass the active niche's `targetBandMinX/MaxX`. |
| `voiceExtract.ts` | `POST /voice/tweets/:tweetId/extract`, `POST /voice/extract-batch` (‚Č§50). LLM-gated mount (**AI.6** `llmConfigured()`). **AI.5:** the ¬ß8.3 prompt/schema moved to pure `../voice/extractPrompt.ts` (registry-cycle avoidance); `extractOne` renders `loadPromptSafe('voice-extract')` via `renderPrompt` and calls `askLLM` (defaults effort low/250 tok/temp 0.2; cache key = `prompt.cacheKey`, no niche suffix ‚ÄĒ no persona in this prompt); failures classify `llm_not_configured`/`grok_<status>`/`openrouter_<status>`. |
| `harvest.ts` | `POST /harvest/runs`, `POST /harvest/rows` (‚Č§500; replies-mode reconcile ‚Üí backfills draft `postedTweetId`), `GET /harvest/runs`. **HV.1** `POST /harvest/passive` (‚Č§100/batch, **$0**, zero schema change): ambient home-timeline rows into the SAME `harvest_rows`, discriminated by `mode='timeline'` and hung off ONE server-created run per UTC day (`{handle:'timeline', mode:'timeline', scope:'passive'}`) ‚ÄĒ `MODES` deliberately still excludes `'timeline'`, so `POST /harvest/runs` keeps rejecting it and clients can never forge a passive run (decision 7). Gates in order: lazy 60d retention prune (`mode='timeline'` only ‚ÄĒ a hand-run harvest of the same age survives) ‚Üí find-or-create today's run (`createdAt >= utcDayStart(now)`) ‚Üí in-batch dedupe by tweetId + 30-min recapture gate (both counted as `skippedRecent`; served by `harvest_rows_tweet_captured_idx`) ‚Üí daily cap 2000 (`skippedCap`) ‚Üí one sync txn insert + `rowCount` bump. Always `201 {runId, inserted, skippedRecent, skippedCap}`. Band is NEVER stored (¬ß7.12 ‚ÄĒ recomputable from views/comments/tweetTime/capturedAt/text); **no person events** (decision 6 ‚ÄĒ timeline exposure is not an interest signal; affinity is the read-time bridge in HV.4). Pure exported `utcDayStart(now)`. **HV.4** `GET /harvest/affinity?days=&limit=&minDays=` (**$0**, static path ‚ÄĒ the router still has no `:param` route, so ¬ß7.20 is a "keep it that way" note, not a live trap) ‚Üí `{days, minDays, authors: AffinityAuthor[]}` where `AffinityAuthor = {handle, distinctDays, sightings, lastSeenAt (ISO), avgViews (rounded), stage: Stage|null, inRoster}`. ONE grouped select over `harvest_rows` **filtered `mode='timeline'`** + `capturedAt >= now‚ąídays`, grouped by handle, `having distinctDays >= minDays`, ordered **distinctDays desc then sightings desc** (a viral thread re-scrolled 20√ó in one afternoon is not affinity), limit. Distinct days = `count(distinct strftime('%Y-%m-%d', captured_at/1000, 'unixepoch'))` ‚ÄĒ **UTC**, matching `utcDayStart` and the panel's `passiveRowsToday`. The `people`/`voice_authors` join happens **in TS** off the ‚Č§`limit` handles (never `in ()` ‚ÄĒ early return when the group-by is empty); handles are lowercased on every side so no `lower()` wrapper is needed. `stage` is null unless a NON-retired people row exists, but `inRoster` counts retired rows too ‚ÄĒ a person you deliberately retired is known, not a fresh candidate to nag about. Params via the shared `intParam` helper: absent ‚Üí default, out of range ‚Üí **clamped** (days 7‚Äď90, limit 1‚Äď50, minDays ‚Č•1), non-positive-integer ‚Üí **400** `invalid_days`/`invalid_limit`/`invalid_min_days`. Own tweets are NOT filtered out (decision 8 ‚ÄĒ filtering is analysis-time). |
| `following.ts` | **GR.1** ‚ÄĒ the $0 following ledger (always mounted; nothing in the file can reach `xFetch`, and unfollowing stays a manual act in the X app). `POST /following/runs` `{}` ‚Üí 201 run row. `POST /following/rows` `{runId, rows[‚Č§500], done?}` ‚Üí 201 `{runId, received, applied, inserted, updated, rowsSeen, complete, reconcile}`: in-batch dedupe by handle (**first occurrence wins** ‚ÄĒ the page renders top-down, so the earliest sighting carries the truest `list_position`), then ONE sync txn (¬ß7.13) inserting fresh handles and updating known ones. **Upsert rules:** `first_seen_at` fill-only; `follows_back` always refreshed; a field the scrape didn't report (`displayName`/`listPosition` null) is left alone, never nulled (¬ß7.11); a `confirmed`/`gone` row seen again is **revived to `active`** (presence is ground truth ‚ÄĒ D99a) but keeps its `first_seen_at` and its `unfollow_marked_at`. **Reconcile fires only on `done:true` AND `rowsSeen > 0`** ‚ÄĒ "unseen" is `last_run_id != runId` (every batch stamps it, so no in-memory set): unseen `active|queued`‚Üí`gone`, unseen `done`‚Üí`confirmed`, **seen `done`‚Üí`queued`** (the one reverse edge: the tick didn't take). A run closed with 0 rows is stamped `completed_at` but **`complete` stays false** (D99b) so it neither reconciles nor counts as a fresh sync. Errors: 400 `invalid_body`/`invalid_run_id`/`invalid_done`/`rows_required` (empty rows are legal ONLY with `done:true` ‚ÄĒ D99c)/`too_many_rows`/indexed `invalid_row`/`invalid_handle`/`invalid_display_name`/`invalid_follows_back`/`invalid_list_position`, 404 `run_not_found`, 409 `run_already_complete`. `GET /following?status=&q=&limit=` ‚Üí `{count, total, lastCompleteRunAt, following}` ‚ÄĒ `q` is `instr()` not LIKE (a handle legitimately contains `_`, which LIKE reads as a wildcard). `PATCH /following/:handle` `{status:'done'}` (**only** from `queued`, stamps `unfollow_marked_at`; anything else 409 `invalid_transition`, unknown status 400, **not idempotent** ‚ÄĒ re-ticking a `done` row 409s) and/or `{keep}` (an independent pin that moves NO status ‚ÄĒ GR.3's queue must filter kept rows out of the batch itself). 400 `empty_patch`/`invalid_keep`, 404 `not_found`. **`GET /following/queue` (GR.3) registers ABOVE `/following/:handle`** (¬ß7.20) ‚ÄĒ the current ordering is already the safe one. |
| `mentions.ts` | `GET /mentions`, `POST /mentions/refresh` (6/day server cap), `PATCH /mentions/:tweetId`. |
| `conversations.ts` | `GET /conversations` (regrouped per read), `PATCH /conversations/:conversationId` (read/snooze/mute ‚Üí `conversation_meta`). |
| `people.ts` | `GET /people`, `GET /people/rankmap` (**before `:handle`**), `GET /people/glance` (**AX.1** ‚ÄĒ timeline-decoration map, **also before `:handle`**; $0: non-retired people + unanswered-mention open-loop counts + `loadTargetHandles()` backfill ‚Üí `{count, map: {handle‚Üí{stage,isTarget,openLoops,lastOutboundAt,lastInboundAt,followersCount}}}`, dates ISO), `GET /people/:handle` (dossier), `PATCH /people/:handle` (only demote path), `POST /people/sightings` (C6 batch ‚Č§50), **`POST /people/engagements`** (**NT.3** ‚ÄĒ C10 notification harvest, $0; body `{engagements:[{kind,handle,targetText?,seenAt}]}` ‚Č§`MAX_ENGAGEMENTS_PER_BATCH`=50 ‚Üí `recordEngagements` counts. Sightings-route validation shape: `invalid_body` / `invalid_engagements` / `too_many_engagements` / per-index `invalid_engagement_{kind,handle,target_text,seen_at}_<i>`. **POST, so the ¬ß7.20 static-vs-`:handle` trap doesn't bite** ‚ÄĒ only `GET /people/:handle` exists. `kind` is whitelisted through `isEngagementKind` ‚ÄĒ that is where the parser's `'other'` dies; `targetText` is **re-forced null for a follow** so a stale extension build can't feed a follower's bio to the target matcher; an invalid handle is passed through and surfaces in `skipped`, never fatal), `POST /people/:handle/events`, `POST /people/:handle/icebreakers` (refuse-before-spend; **AI.6** migrated to `askLLM` via `loadPromptSafe('icebreaker')` + `llmErrorPayload`, gate `llmConfigured()` keeping the 503 `grok_not_configured` string; 404‚Üí422‚Üí503 ladder order preserved). |

| `radar.ts` | `GET /radar/drafts?status=&tweetId=` (**RU.5** `?tweetId=` filter: explicit `status` wins, else tweetId‚Üínon-expired, else the ready default; lazy 48h expiry), `PATCH /radar/drafts` (status ratchet), `PATCH /radar/drafts/:tweetId/tags`, **`POST /radar/drafts/:tweetId/confirm` (RU.5)** ‚ÄĒ promotes the newest live radar draft to a measured `reply_drafts` row ($0, always-mounted): idempotent via the soft `reply_draft_id` link (linked row ‚Üí 200; dangling ‚Üí rebuild), else one sync txn (¬ß7.13) inserts `{source:'radar', status:'copied', variants (fallback `[{text:replyText,angle}]`), model `?? 'radar-batch'`, costUsd:null, contextSnapshot=`PostContext` rebuilt from snippet/band+signals/`postedAt=draftedAt‚ąíageMin`}` + stamps `reply_draft_id` + ratchets radar status‚Üí`clicked`; 400 `invalid_tweet_id`, 404 `not_found`. No `my_reply` event here ‚ÄĒ that stays on the PATCH `/replies/:id` posted flip. `copied‚Üíposted` already in `ALLOWED_TRANSITIONS`. **RU.8:** `RadarBatchTweet`/`RadarDraftInsert` band widened to `'manual'`; the confirm endpoint **coerces `band:'manual'`‚Üí`null`** in the rebuilt `contextSnapshot.signals.band` (queue metadata, never a classifier verdict ‚Üí never a Playbook hot/warm cell, ¬ß7.19). |
| `replyLists.ts` | **RL.2** ‚ÄĒ canned-reply list CRUD ($0, always mounted next to `ideasRouter`). `GET /reply-lists` (sortOrder asc, each row + `itemCount`/`enabledCount` from ONE grouped select), `POST /reply-lists` (`{name ‚Č§120, description? ‚Č§2000, humanizer?, active?, sortOrder?}`), `GET /reply-lists/:id` ‚Üí `{list, items}` (items createdAt asc), `PATCH /reply-lists/:id` (partial, `empty_patch` 400), `DELETE /reply-lists/:id` (items cascade via FK; the use log survives on purpose), `POST /reply-lists/:id/items` (`{mode:'append'|'replace', items:[{text}] ‚Č§100 each 1..`MAX_REPLY_LENGTH`, source?:'manual'|'ai'}` ‚ÄĒ ONE sync txn ¬ß7.13, replace = delete+insert, response is always the list's WHOLE current set so both modes read alike; `createdAt` stamped per row past the list's current max so insertion order survives a same-millisecond batch), `PATCH/DELETE /reply-lists/:id/items/:itemId` (**both scoped `id` AND `listId`** ‚ÄĒ right item under the wrong list is a 404). `humanizer` runs through the engine's `parseHumanizerConfig` and is stored NORMALIZED: `null` clears to `DEFAULT_HUMANIZER`, a non-object ‚Üí 400 `invalid_humanizer`, a partially-bad object is lenient-parsed and accepted (D76a). Malformed uuid ‚Üí 400 `invalid_id`, well-formed-but-absent ‚Üí 404 (ideas.ts idiom). **RL.3** `POST /reply-lists/:id/use` (`{vars?:{name?,handle?} ‚Č§120, targetTweetId? /^\d{1,32}$/, targetHandle? (normalized no-`@`/lowercase, `USERNAME_RE`), preview?}` ‚Üí `{itemId, text, missingVars, applied}`): loads ALL items (pickItem owns the enabled/var rules ‚ÄĒ one place), `pickItem(items, availableVarsFor(vars), Math.random)` ‚Üí **409 `no_enabled_items`** when null, `composeReply(item.text, vars, resolveHumanizer(list.humanizer), Math.random)` (protected spans come from the vars inside composeReply ‚ÄĒ there is no `protectedValues` arg), then unless `preview` ONE sync txn stamps `lastUsedAt` + `use_count+1` and inserts the `reply_list_uses` row. **`lastUsedAt` is stamped monotonically past the list's max** (¬ß7.13a ‚ÄĒ the anti-repeat window only holds while the just-used item is STRICTLY most recent); `updatedAt` deliberately untouched (it means "text edited"). A body-less POST is a legal no-target use; a body that parses to a non-object 400s. An `active:false` list is still usable (active is presentation state, not a gate). **RL.4** `POST /reply-lists/:id/generate` (`{prompt 1..2000, count? 1..30 default 12, model?, provider?}` ‚Üí `{items:[{text}], count, requested, model, costUsd, requestId}`): the only non-$0 route here ‚ÄĒ one `askLLM` structured-outputs call (defaults temp 0.9 / 1500 tok / low, `promptCacheKey` = the bare registry sha) that **writes NOTHING** (Decision 3 ‚ÄĒ the panel previews and the user applies via `POST /items` `source:'ai'`, so "overwrite my list" stays a human click). Guard order: `invalid_id` ‚Üí `invalid_body` ‚Üí `invalid_prompt` ‚Üí `invalid_count` (**refused, not clamped** ‚ÄĒ silently returning 12 of 40 reads as broken) ‚Üí `invalid_model`/`invalid_provider` ‚Üí **404 before any spend** ‚Üí existing item texts (disabled included) into the prompt tail. **No pre-flight key check** (ideas.ts/AI.9 precedent, D80): `askLLM` enforces the resolved provider's key and `llmErrorPayload` maps it ‚Üí 503 `llm_not_configured` ‚ÄĒ NOT `grok_not_configured`, so an OpenRouter-only setup works; parse null ‚Üí 502 `items_parse_error`, `[]` ‚Üí 502 `items_invalid`. |
| `ideas.ts` | `GET/POST /ideas`, `PATCH /ideas/:id` (consume/reopen provenance rules), `DELETE /ideas/:id`. **AI.9:** `POST /ideas/generate {steer?, count? (1‚Äď10, default 8), model?, provider?}` ‚Üí `{ideas:[{text,pillar,angle}], count, requested, costUsd, model}` ‚ÄĒ **writes nothing** (the panel saves picked ones via `POST /ideas` `tags:['ai']`); pre-spend guards `invalid_body`/`invalid_steer` [‚Č§2000]/`invalid_count`/`invalid_model`/`invalid_provider` (400) then `getActivePillars()` empty ‚Üí **409 `no_pillars_for_niche`** (drafter discipline ‚ÄĒ a custom niche with no pillars never spends nor leaks builder pillars); `topWinners()` few-shot (imported from `drafter.ts` ‚ÄĒ deferred function call, safe cycle) + `loadPromptSafe('ideas')` ‚Üí `askLLM` (defaults temp 0.8/1400 tok/low, cache key = bare `prompt.cacheKey`, **no niche suffix** ‚ÄĒ persona-free prompt, pillars at the tail); `parseIdeaProposals` null ‚Üí 502 `ideas_parse_error`, `[]` ‚Üí 502 `ideas_invalid`, `llmErrorPayload` ‚Üí 503 `llm_not_configured`. |

Extension `ChannelTags` + content-script chips inherit the filter with zero client change. |
| `playbook.ts` | `GET /playbook?minN=`, `POST /playbook/extract-winners` (‚Č§20 winners/call, runtime `llmConfigured()` check ‚Üí 503 `grok_not_configured` AI.6; **AI.5** shares `loadPromptSafe('voice-extract')` + `renderPrompt` with voiceExtract's path, `askLLM`, body `provider` accepted). Loaders + `loadReplyGuidanceSafe`/`loadPostGuidanceSafe` (always DEFAULT gate) + exported `loadFollowersByHandle`. **ME.5:** `ReplyRow.hasMe` (from `ctx.me`) feeds `meEffectiveness` in the payload ‚ÄĒ no new query, same reply rows as relationship lift. **RU.9:** `loadOriginRows` selects `replyDrafts.source` alongside `postedTweetId` and builds the `postedTweetId‚Üísource` map fed to `classifyReplyOrigin` (exact radar attribution, text-match only as the no-draft-link fallback). **RL.7:** one more unwindowed select ‚ÄĒ every `reply_list_uses.renderedText` normalized into a `Set` (empty strings skipped) ‚ÄĒ feeds the `canned` bucket; the table is FK-free so a deleted list never erases its attribution. **HV.5:** `loadTimelineFunnel(minN)` ‚Üí `timelineFunnel` in the payload ‚ÄĒ ONE grouped select over `harvest_rows` **filtered `mode='timeline'`** + `capturedAt >= now‚ąí30d`, `min(captured_at)` with bare columns (SQLite's documented first-sighting form: with exactly one min/max aggregate every bare column comes from the matching row) `group by tweet_id`, then the posted-`reply_drafts.sourceTweetId` set intersected against it. Window is 30d (shorter than the 60d passive retention on purpose) and **unlimited by design** ‚ÄĒ volume is structurally bounded by HV.1's 2,000-rows/day cap, and a `limit` would truncate the denominator. $0. |

## 4. Database ‚ÄĒ 36 tables

`src/db/shared-schema.ts`: **cost_events** (platform-tagged spend ledger) ¬∑ **app_settings** (UI.1 ‚ÄĒ settings overrides; key PK, JSON value, `updatedAt`; only overridden keys get a row).

`src/x/db/schema.ts` (schema line numbers as of stamp):

| Table | Purpose / notes |
|---|---|
| `tokens` (L14) | Single row `id='default'` OAuth tokens. Excluded from explorer/MCP entirely. |
| `contentPillars` (L33) | Editable pillars; seed INSERT lives in migration 0000. Never let the active set go empty (409 guards). **N0.1** adds nullable `niche` (backfilled `'builder'`, migration 0015). |
| `channels` (L54) | C8 topic rooms: slug PK, keywords JSON, optional pillar link (not FK-validated). **N0.1** adds nullable `niche` (backfilled `'builder'`). |
| `niches` (L70) | **N0.1** ‚ÄĒ first-class identity container: slug PK, `persona`/`beliefs`/`replyPersona` (prompt-grounding, lifted verbatim from post ¬ß1/¬ß5 + reply "Who I am"), `description`, `doctrine` JSON (null=defaults), `active` (exactly one, v1). Seeded `builder` mirroring `DEFAULT_NICHE` byte-for-byte (migration 0015). **INERT until N0.3/N0.4/N0.5** wire consumers. |
| `mediaAssets` (L77) | S4 Studio PNGs as BLOBs (kind, prompt, w/h, usedOnTweetId). `assets.ts` `ASSET_KINDS` whitelist widened (**S5.5**) to all S5 template ids ‚ÄĒ `quote/stat/banner/pfp/milestone/streak/code/thread/list/chart/background/other`; unknown ‚Üí `'other'`. |
| `scheduledPosts` (L94) | Calendar. status `draft\|pending\|publishing\|posted\|failed\|cancelled\|segment`; `thread_id`, `position`, `quote_tweet_id`, `pillar`, `register`, `media_note`, `source`. `publishing`/`posted` worker-owned. |
| `postsPublished` (L139) | Everything actually posted (incl. app-made): `in_reply_to_tweet_id`, `conversation_id`, `has_media` (null=unknown, never "no"). |
| `metricsSnapshots` (L164) | Once-only snapshots; `age_at_snapshot_min`; joined newest-first-wins everywhere. |
| `postTemplates` (L189) | C4 extracted winner structures (hook/skeleton/device, lowercased keys). |
| `accountSnapshots` (L205) | Daily getMe KPI, 1/UTC-day, + `pinned_tweet_id` (S0.9). Latest row = "my size" for banding. |
| `voiceAuthors` (L225) / `voiceAuthorSnapshots` (L253) / `voiceTweets` (L268) | Swipe file (DOM-scraped, $0): profile + follower series (append per enrich) + tweets (`scraped_html`, template columns from ¬ß8.3, `tags`). |
| `replyDrafts` (L301) | Grok reply drafts: `variants` JSON, `source` (RU.2 ‚ÄĒ `'reply_master'\|'radar'`, null=legacy), `contextSnapshot` (records exactly what the model saw ‚ÄĒ signals, relationship, guidance), `postedTweetId` (the outcome join key), `idea`, `pillar`. `updatedAt` of posted flip = paste time. |
| `radarDrafts` (L357) | C0 persisted batch replies; status `ready\|clicked\|expired` ratchet; 48h lazy expiry; `tags`; RU.2 adds `variants` JSON, `model`, `reply_draft_id` (soft link, no FK); **RU.3** `buildRadarDraftRows` stores `r.variants` from the batch (null when a CLI/smoke caller passes only the primary text/angle); **RU.5** `POST ‚Ä¶/confirm` writes `reply_draft_id` + ratchets status‚Üí`clicked` when a draft is promoted to a `reply_drafts` row; **RU.8** the `band` column now also stores `'manual'` (a ‚äē pinned tweet), coerced away from the confirmed reply snapshot's classifier signals. |
| `people` (L397) / `personEvents` (L428) / `personSnapshots` (L449) | C1 CRM: handle PK + stage + watermarks; append-only timeline (**deterministic ids** `type:ref_table:ref_id`, INSERT OR IGNORE); ambient follower series (C6 hover, once/day gates). **NT.2 (comment-only, no migration):** `type` is free text ‚ÄĒ its comment now lists `their_like`/`their_repost`/`their_follow`; `source` lists `hover`/`launch`/`notification` (the old list was already stale). |
| `ideas` (L470) | C6 Idea Inbox: status `open\|consumed\|discarded`, consume provenance (`consumed_by_table/-id` restricted to reply_drafts/scheduled_posts). |
| `followupSnoozes` (L496) | item_key `kind:handle` or `reup:<tweetId>`. |
| `streaks` (L509) | Local-day PK diary (C9); upserted by brief reads. |
| `digests` (L522) | Weekly digest cache (week_key PK). |
| `mentions` (L542) | Inbox; **max stored tweet_id IS the since_id checkpoint** ‚ÄĒ never insert non-API ids; status flow + `answered_draft_id`. **Two DOM surfaces route around this trap:** C7 `launch.ts` (early repliers ‚Üí person events only) and NT.5's notifications surface (reads mention rows for parent context, writes none ‚ÄĒ the freshness gap is closed by the human sync chip, not by inserting scraped ids). |
| `conversationMeta` (L568) | C2 snooze/read/mute per conversation_id. |
| `harvestRuns` (L630) / `harvestRows` (L643) | DOM harvest; repeated captures on purpose (longitudinal series); content-shape columns; index `(tweet_id, captured_at)`. **HV.1 added NO column and NO migration** ‚ÄĒ `mode`/`scope` are free-text, so passive rows are `mode='timeline'` + `scope='passive'` on existing fields (orig\*/`group_position`/`matched_draft_id` null). The only other reader, `scripts/backfill-people.ts`, filters `mode='replies'`, so passive rows can't pollute it ‚ÄĒ **any new consumer MUST filter on `mode`**. Readers of the `mode='timeline'` corpus so far: `GET /harvest/affinity` (HV.4) and `loadTimelineFunnel` in `routes/playbook.ts` (HV.5). |
| `meEntries` (L689) | **ME.1** Me profile: `kind` (fact/event/emotion/note), `text`, `happened_at` (null=undated ‚Üí created_at drives windows), `pinned`/`active`. No seed (empty = byte-identical prompts). |
| `meGoals` (L711) | **ME.1** Measurable goals: `kind` (followers/mrr/custom), `target`, `unit`, `current_value` (manual for mrr/custom; followers auto ‚Üź account_snapshots), `deadline`, `status` (active/achieved/dropped). D4: GR.7 extends this, not a second table. |
| `replyLists` (L757) / `replyListItems` (L777) / `replyListUses` (L809) | **RL.2** Canned reply lists: list (`humanizer` JSON, null = engine defaults, stored NORMALIZED through `parseHumanizerConfig`) ‚Üí items (template `text`, `enabled`, `source` manual/ai, **`last_used_at`/`use_count` = the server-side anti-repeat state**, FK `list_id` **ON DELETE CASCADE**, index `(list_id, last_used_at)` = exactly what `pickItem`'s recency window reads) ‚Üí uses (the audit log AND the Playbook `canned` measurement hook via a normalized `rendered_text` match; **deliberately NOT FK'd** so the history outlives an edited-away item or a deleted list; index `(used_at)`). Migration 0018, DDL-only, no seed. |
| `followingRuns` (L836) / `following` (L862) | **GR.1** Following ledger from ONE $0 DOM scrape of my own `/following` page (X renders a "Follows you" badge per row, so one pass yields both sides ‚ÄĒ no API sync, no `follows.write` scope). Run: `started_at`/`completed_at`/`rows_seen`/**`complete`** ‚ÄĒ the trust flag, since only a run that walked the WHOLE list may conclude anything from a handle's absence. Ledger: handle PK (lowercased), `display_name`, `follows_back` (notNull ‚ÄĒ the badge's absence IS the "no", there is no third state), `list_position` (render order ‚Čą follow recency, a tie-break not a date), `first_seen_at` **fill-only** (the follow-date proxy ¬ß7.11 ‚ÄĒ `followed_at` deliberately doesn't exist), `last_seen_at`, `last_run_id` FK, `status` (active\|queued\|done\|confirmed\|gone), `keep` (manual never-suggest pin), `unfollow_marked_at` (**never cleared** ‚ÄĒ the 6h/24h churn budgets count marks in a trailing window). Index `(status, first_seen_at)` = exactly GR.3's eligibility query. |
| `promptOverrides` (L748) | **AI.3** Editable-prompt OVERRIDE ROWS ONLY (key = registry `PromptKey`, body, updatedAt). Row absent = the shipped default in `prompts/registry.ts` applies; restore = DELETE; `customized` = row presence. No seed by design (a later-deploy default improvement applies unless overridden). Explorer/MCP-visible ‚ÄĒ never store secrets. |

Migrations `0000`‚Äď`0019` (latest: `0019_messy_blue_shield` GR.1 `following`+`following_runs` ‚ÄĒ 2 CREATE TABLEs + 1 index, DDL-only, no seed, nothing touched on existing tables. `following` is created BEFORE the `following_runs` it FKs to; SQLite resolves FK targets at DML time, not CREATE time, so the order is harmless. `0018_flimsy_captain_universe` RL.2 `reply_lists`+`reply_list_items`+`reply_list_uses` ‚ÄĒ 3 CREATE TABLEs + 2 indexes, DDL-only, no seed, nothing touched on existing tables; `0013` app_settings, `0014` RU.2 reply `source` + radar `variants`/`model`/`reply_draft_id`, `0015` N0.1 `niches` table + seed INSERT + nullable `niche` on content_pillars/channels + `UPDATE ‚Ä¶ SET niche='builder'` backfills ‚ÄĒ the seed/backfill DML was hand-appended after generate, `0016_high_miek` ME.1 `me_entries`+`me_goals` ‚ÄĒ DDL-only, no seed, `0017_misty_zeigeist` AI.3 `prompt_overrides` ‚ÄĒ single CREATE TABLE, no seed by design). Workflow: edit schema ‚Üí `bun run db:generate` ‚Üí **inspect the SQL** (drizzle drops seed INSERTs; keep them idempotent) ‚Üí boot/`deploy.sh` migrates. (biome now ignores `src/db/migrations` ‚ÄĒ UI.1, D11/D13.)

## 5. Extension ‚ÄĒ `extension/` (own package.json, Vite + React, MV3)

**Build:** two passes (`vite.config.ts`) ‚ÄĒ content script first as self-contained **IIFE** (`content.js`; classic script, no imports allowed), then side panel + background as ES modules. Shared modules used by content.ts get inlined. Out-of-tree server modules reach the extension via **re-export shims**: `extension/src/replyBand.ts` ‚Üí `src/shared/replyBand.ts`, `extension/src/channelSuggest.ts` ‚Üí `src/shared/channelSuggest.ts` (tsconfig lists them in `include`).

**Manifest:** side panel + background service worker + content script on x.com/twitter.com. Permissions: sidePanel, storage, clipboardWrite/Read, contextMenus, alarms, notifications.

| File | Purpose |
|---|---|
| `src/background.ts` | Service worker. **Single writer of all `chrome.storage.session` state** (radar ring buffer cap 100 + dismissed cap 500, launch room state), writes serialized via promise chain. One HTTP transport: `ApiRequest` message channel ‚ÄĒ the only Authorization-header owner (incl. `binary` for asset blobs). Rankmap cache (10min TTL, S0.3). C7 launch alarms (`chrome.alarms`, +90s grace, liveness verify, notification). Ideas context menu. **RU.6** `stratus/radar-confirm` handler ‚Üí `confirmDraft(tweetId)` POSTs `/x/radar/drafts/:id/confirm` (best-effort ¬ß7.8; ignores `unconfigured`) then `stampDraftId` writes the returned reply_drafts `id` onto the sighting (single writer, markClicked pattern). **RU.7** `stratus/radar-variants-get`‚Üí`getVariants` (session buffer `isReplyVariants(hit.variants)` first, else `GET /x/radar/drafts?tweetId=` ‚Üí newest row's `.drafts[0]`, variants ?? `[{text:replyText, angle}]`) returns `{variants, draftId}|null`; `stratus/radar-variant-pasted`‚Üí`pasteVariant` POSTs the idempotent confirm (covers deep links) then PATCHes `/x/replies/:id {status:'posted', replyTextEdited?}` ‚ÄĒ the confirm response IS the reply_drafts row so its `replyText` is the primary (chosen text ‚Č† primary ‚Üí `replyTextEdited`); best-effort ¬ß7.8, warn-only. **AX.6** `stratus/open-person`‚Üí`chrome.sidePanel.open({tabId: sender.tab?.id})` [best-effort user-gesture, one-hop] + writes the `stratus:openPerson` session handoff key `{handle, at}` via its own `enqueueOpenPerson` chain [single writer]; `stratus/open-person-clear`‚Üíremoves the key. **NT.4** notifications context: `NOTIF_CONTEXT_TTL_MS`=5min + `notifContext`/`notifContextAt`/`notifContextInflight` (rankmap-cache idiom; only a successful pull advances the stamp) ‚ÄĒ `refreshNotifContext()` GETs `/x/mentions?limit=200` and maps rows to `{parentText, status}` by reply `tweetId`; `stratus/notif-context`‚Üí`notifContextPayload(force)` awaits `refreshNotifContext`+`refreshRankMap` in parallel (both TTL-guarded no-ops) ‚Üí `{ok:true, mentions, rankMap}`, and on `force` it drains any in-flight refresh THEN invalidates (a sync click must not be answered by a pull that started before it). **Always `ok:true`** ‚ÄĒ every failure path degrades to the last-good/empty map. |
| `src/content.ts` | On-page: reply-band **border/dim** (`readTweetSignals`; **AX.3** the green stats *badge* is gone ‚ÄĒ border/dim + `recordRadarSighting` byte-identical, radar stream untouched) + **AX.3 person chips** (`applyPersonChips(article, glance)` from `scan` decorates the `[data-testid="User-Name"]` line via `buildPersonChips` over a `GET /people/glance` `GLANCE_TTL_MS` module cache [channels pattern; sync `getGlanceMap`‚Üíbg `refreshGlanceMap`, `unconfigured` silent], recompute-per-scan `data-handle`+`data-sig` skip-guard, chip `<button>`s carry `data-tone`/`data-handle`, **AX.6** click ‚Üí `sendOpenPerson(handle)` [preventDefault+stopPropagation so X never navigates]; `.finally`‚Üí`scheduleScan()` since a status page can be mutation-quiet], renders `buildTweetContextModel` [AX.4] into `div.stratus-context-panel` inserted as the article's **next sibling** [`insertAdjacentElement('afterend')`, not cloned on recycle], `data-renderKey` [state:tweetId:handle:cachedAt] rebuild guard + SPA-nav teardown; header stage chip reuses `.stratus-person-chip[data-tone]`, collapse toggle `‚Ėĺ`/`‚Ėł` persisted to `chrome.storage.local['augment:contextCollapsed']` [`initContextCollapsed`], 404‚Üíone muted line, unconfigured‚Üínothing; each chip a `<button>` [angle label + `variantChipPreview(text)`, `title`=full text]; click ‚Üí `clearReplyEditor` [selectAll+delete only if non-empty] + `typeTextInto(findReplyEditor())` [clipboard fallback + hint], mark `data-active`, then `stratus/radar-variant-pasted {tweetId, text}` ‚ÄĒ posting stays manual ¬ß7.28), save-to-stratus + save-author scrape, radar sightings stream (2s flush/60s throttle), **RU.8 ‚äē manual add** (`attachRadarAddButton` from `scan` on every action row ‚ÄĒ `radarAddHandled` WeakSet + `attachButton` discipline; click ‚Üí `onRadarAddClick` builds a `band:'manual'` sighting [`readTweetSignals` or `synthManualSignals` zeros + timestamp-derived ageMin], flips ‚úď optimistically, sends `stratus/radar-report` **immediately** [one deliberate click, not batched] ‚ÄĒ the background stays the single buffer writer ¬ß7.24), C6 passive hover capture, C7 early-replies stream + launch-get throttle, post-save channel chips, `metrics_unparsed` loud error, **NT.5 notifications surface** (one `onNotificationsPage()` pathname gate computed once per `scan` ‚ÄĒ X navigates without reloads, so it is per-scan, never once: (a) `applyNotifParentContext(article)` inside the article loop injects `‚Ü≥ on your post: ‚Äú‚Ä¶‚ÄĚ ‚úď answered` under `[data-testid="tweetText"]` [article-append fallback for a media-only reply], keyed by `findPermalink().tweetId` ‚ÄĒ **live-verified that this yields the REPLY's own id, exactly how `NotifContextMap` is keyed** ‚ÄĒ `data-sig` guarded, removes itself when a recycled node no longer matches, and **renders on `answered` alone even with a null `parentText`** [the don't-reply-twice signal]; (b) `applyNotifTierChips(cell, handles)` puts up to 3 `personTierFor(rankMap[h])` chips **after** the header `[dir]` block ‚ÄĒ tweet-articles already get the richer AX.3 glance chips, so this covers only the aggregated cells;
