Context via `syncNotifContext()` [60s throttle, in-flight guarded, stamped **on settle not on success** so a failing ask can't re-fire every frame; the forced variant deliberately bypasses that guard so a sync click is never swallowed] ‚Üí `scheduleScan()` on arrival, since the page goes mutation-quiet). **HV.2 passive timeline harvest** (`recordPassiveHarvest(article)`, called from `applyBand` for EVERY parseable band incl. `skip` ‚ÄĒ the funnel needs the denominator, and a null `sig` is an ad/promoted row that filters itself): gates in cost order ‚ÄĒ `passiveHarvestEnabled` (the `passiveHarvest` key, default ON, `initPassiveCaptureSetting` listener pattern) ‚Üí `isHomeTimelinePath(location.pathname)` **re-read per call** (X navigates without reloading) ‚Üí `!isHarvestActive()` ‚Üí `findPermalink` (ONE querySelector) ‚Üí pending/throttle maps ‚Üí only THEN `extractArticle` (harvester's reader, ¬ß7.27 ‚ÄĒ not a second parser). `flushPassiveHarvest` mirrors `flushSightings`: 5s window, ‚Č§100/batch with overflow re-arm, `passiveSentAt` cleared past 5000, `ApiRequest POST /x/harvest/passive`, `unconfigured` ignored, everything else warn-and-**drop** (never retried ‚ÄĒ a lost sighting is a missing point on a view curve, not a lost user action). |
| `src/harvester.ts` | Timeline harvester (human-like scroll, aria metric parse, CSV + ingest rows, since-last cursors) ‚ÄĒ driven over a port from the Harvest tab; imported by content.ts. **HV.2 exports three things for the passive capture:** `interface Extracted`, `extractArticle(art)` (the ONE DOM reader), and `isHarvestActive()` over the module-level `running` flag (a hand-run harvest owns the scroll ‚Üí passive capture suspends). **HV.3:** `HarvestCtx.minViews` threads `options.minViews` into `harvestPosts`/`harvestReplies`, applied **after `noteSeen`** (a filtered item still counts as scrolled-past ‚ÄĒ otherwise a high floor defeats the day-window exhaustion break and scrolls to `HARD_STEP_CAP`) and before the store write, so the floor reaches the CSV and the ingest alike; `options.downloadCsv === false` skips `download()` and emits `filename: ''` on the `done` event (the panel's only signal for "saved to stratus only"). |
| `src/shared/` | `messages.ts` (all message types: `stratus/api`, radar-\*, launch-\*; **RU.4** `RadarReplies.replies[]` carries optional `variants` alongside the primary `reply`; **RU.6** `RadarConfirm {type:'stratus/radar-confirm', tweetId}` + `isRadarConfirm` guard ‚ÄĒ bun-tested in `messages.test.ts`; **prefixes VERIFIED against live x.com/notifications in NT.5** ‚ÄĒ like `M20.884 13.19` (filled heart, 191 live cells) + `M16.697 5.5` (outline heart, the action-row asset), repost `M4.5 3.88` (verified by asset identity with the live action-row retweet icon ‚ÄĒ no repost cell was in the window), follow **corrected** from the wrong `M12 11.816` to `M17.863 13.44` (14 live cells); the bell glyph `M11.996 2c` is deliberately unmapped so "New post notifications for ‚Ä¶ and 6 others" cells fall to `'other'` and get dropped; an unrecognised glyph still degrades to keywords, never to `'other'`], then en+ro verb stems over the first `[dir]` header block, then the whole cell text, checked **like ‚Üí repost ‚Üí follow** so the loose `urmńÉre` stem is only reachable when the like/repost phrases failed; dependency-free for the content IIFE; 12 bun tests), `metricsAria.ts` (locale-hardened), `harvest.ts`, `bgClient.ts`, **`aiSettings.ts`** (AI.10 ‚ÄĒ pure `aiSettingsToForm`/`aiFormToPatch` [form fields are strings so blank is representable ‚Üí explicit null; Consumes the C1 dossier `GET /people/:handle` as HTTP JSON [all timestamps ISO strings]; pure `buildTweetContextModel(dossier, tweetId, nowMs) ‚Üí {header, relationship, alreadyReplied, openLoops, outcomes, anglePreference, notes}`: header stage/sinceDays[firstSeenAt]/followers/`momentumPerDay`[followerSeries clamp ‚Č•1 day, mirrors `authorMomentum`, null <2 pts]/tags; relationship inbound/outbound COUNTS from `events` [their_mention+their_reply_to_me vs my_reply], last dates from the `people` watermarks; `alreadyReplied` = a posted outcome whose `sourceTweetId===tweetId` [ageMin off `postedAt ?? draftCreatedAt`]; openLoops = unanswered `mentions` oldest-first; outcomes = measured-only reply outcomes newest-first ‚Č§3 [angle optional ‚ÄĒ the dossier does NOT emit per-outcome angle today, reads null]; `anglePreference` mirrors `pickAnglePreference` [gate total-measured‚Č•3=`MIN_MEASURED_FOR_ANGLE_PREFERENCE`, best median profileVisits, views tie-break]; notes trimmed. Null-safe for hover-only people; dependency-free for the content IIFE; 15 bun tests. **AX.5** consumed LIVE by content.ts `syncContextPanel`/`renderContextPanel`), **`variantChips.ts`** (RU.7 ‚ÄĒ pure `variantChipPreview(text, max=60)` [collapse whitespace ‚Üí clip with `‚Ä¶`, never exceeds max] + `isReplyVariants(v)` [shape guard: NON-empty array of `{text, angle}`, angle a loose string ‚ÄĒ looser-client-cache tolerance]; the two testable bits of the on-page chips, since content.ts is untested by convention; consumed by content.ts `syncVariantChips` + background `getVariants`; 7 bun tests). **NT.4** `messages.ts` gained the C10 pair `NotifContextGet {type:'stratus/notif-context', force?}` + `isNotifContextGet`, plus the exported response shape `NotifContextResponse {ok:true, mentions: NotifContextMap, rankMap}` where `NotifContextMap = Record<replyTweetId, {parentText, status: MentionStatus}>` ‚ÄĒ NT.5 casts its `sendMessage` to that type instead of hand-writing the structure (+2 guard tests in `messages.test.ts`). **HV.2** `passiveHarvest.ts` ‚ÄĒ pure core of the passive capture: `PASSIVE_HARVEST_KEY`/`PASSIVE_FLUSH_MS=5000`/`PASSIVE_RESEND_MS=30min`/`PASSIVE_BATCH_MAX=100`/`PASSIVE_TEXT_MAX=500` (the last three mirror the server's `MAX_PASSIVE_BATCH`/`PASSIVE_RECAPTURE_MS` so the wire carries no row the server would only count as `skippedRecent`), `isHomeTimelinePath` (exactly `/home`, trailing-slash tolerant), `shouldRecordPassive`, and `toPassiveIngestRow(x: Extracted): HarvestIngestRow|null` (null when the permalink didn't resolve; text clamped to 500 but `textLen` = PRE-truncation length; `time: x.time || null` ‚ÄĒ never `''`). Type-only `import type { Extracted } from '../harvester.ts'` (erased: `verbatimModuleSyntax`), so the pure module keeps zero runtime deps. **HV.3** `harvest.ts` (previously wire-format + URL helpers only, and untested) gained its first suite plus three pure exports: `passesMinViews(views, minViews?)` (absent/NaN/‚Č§0 ‚Üí passes everything), the persisted-form trio `HARVEST_FORM_KEY='harvestForm'`/`HarvestForm`/`DEFAULT_HARVEST_FORM` + `parseHarvestForm(raw)` (field-by-field lenient parse per `parseBrandKit`; `maxStr`/`minViewsStr` are the raw **digit strings** the panel holds, so a blank box round-trips as blank instead of collapsing to a 0 floor), and `passiveRowsToday(runs, nowMs)` + `PASSIVE_RUN_MODE='timeline'` (sums today's timeline runs off `GET /x/harvest/runs`; the boundary is **UTC** to match the server's `utcDayStart` ‚ÄĒ a local-midnight window would read yesterday's run for part of every day). Type-only `import type { HarvestRun } from './types.ts'` (erased ‚ÄĒ verified absent from the content IIFE bundle). |

export/import round-trips both file shapes via `parseBrandKitsFile`. The **S5.4 background segmented control** (`gradient|dots|grid|diagonal|plus|blobs|AI image` + blobs reroll; picking a pattern clears the AI bitmap) lives inline in `Studio.tsx`, not fields.tsx. **Adding a template = 1 registry row + 1 field section**, not another shell branch. |
| `src/sidepanel/styles.css` | The panel stylesheet (~2.4k lines). **UI.8:** `:root` holds the full `--strat-*` design-token set (verbatim from `Stratus Design System/tokens/*.css`) + `--x-*` companion tokens + **legacy short aliases** (`--bg: var(--strat-bg)` ‚Ä¶) the sheet still resolves through. **Zero color literals outside `:root`** ‚ÄĒ tinted fills use exact fill tokens (`--strat-{accent,danger,warn}-fill`, `--strat-pillar-bg`, `--strat-scrim`) or `color-mix(in srgb, var(--strat-*) N%, transparent)` (exact-equivalent, and tracks the base so Task-9 light theme flows through). Inter is `@font-face`d from `/fonts/` and set on `body` via `--strat-font-sans`; metric classes get `tabular-nums`. **UI.9:** `:root[data-theme='light']` re-tints by redefining only the base `--strat-*` tokens (aliases resolve lazily ‚Üí whole sheet flows through; `color-scheme: light`; direct-use fill tokens + band ink re-authored for a light base, dark text companions kept); density via `[data-density='compact']` and scale via `[data-scale='12'|'14']` override the new `--ui-panel-pad`/`--ui-section-gap`/`--ui-row-gap`/`--ui-root-size` vars that `body`/`.panel`/`.row` now consume. **UI.10:** `.brand`/`.brand-mark`/`.brand-word` + `.tab-group`/`.tab-group-eyebrow` (grouped rail), and a tail `.ui-*` block for the primitives (Section/EmptyState/SubTabs/SettingRow/Slider/GearPopover) ‚ÄĒ `--strat-*` tokens only, no literals. **RL.5:** a tail `.rl-*` block (rail/detail/items/chances/testvars/preview/proposals) ‚ÄĒ same rule, `color-mix` over `--strat-accent` for the selected rail chip; everything else leans on `.pillar-card*`/`.field`/`.row`/`.status-line`. **RL.6:** a tail `.quick-reply*` block (relative wrapper + absolutely-positioned `right:0` popover card, list rows, result/status/meta/err) ‚ÄĒ `--strat-*` tokens only, no literals; the status line flips to `--strat-warn` via `.quick-reply-status-warn` when the clipboard refused. |
| `public/fonts/` | Bundled Inter WOFF2s (Regular/Bold/ExtraBold) + **S5.6** JetBrains Mono WOFF2s (Regular/Bold, OFL-1.1, latin subset) ‚ÄĒ served at `/fonts/`, loaded by the Studio (`studio/fonts.ts`, FontFace: Inter‚Üí`StudioInter`, Mono‚Üí`StudioMono`) and the panel sheet (`@font-face`, UI.8). |
| Storage keys | `chrome.storage.local`: brand kit, settings toggles (**HV.2 `passiveHarvest`** ‚ÄĒ default ON/opt-out, absent key = enabled; read directly by content.ts AND through `sidepanel/storage.ts`'s `Settings` ‚ÄĒ HV.3 added the key to `useSettings`'s `onChanged` filter, which HV.2 had missed, so a toggle now reaches the panel tree live), harvest cursors, **HV.3 `harvestForm`** (the whole Harvest-tab form in one blob; `harvestSendToStratus` stays separate), `replyMaster:idea(+Id)`, **AX.5 `augment:contextCollapsed`** (tweet-page context-panel collapse state), **UI.9 appearance `theme`/`density`/`uiScale`** (stamped on `<html>` by `main.tsx` as `data-theme`/`data-density`/`data-scale`; `system` resolved via `matchMedia`). `chrome.storage.session`: `radar:sightings`, `radar:dismissed`, `launch:active`, `launch:replies`, **AX.6 `stratus:openPerson`** (`{handle, at}` dossier-open handoff ‚ÄĒ background-written single writer, App.tsx consumes on mount + `onChanged` then clears via `stratus/open-person-clear`). |

## 6. MCP + integrations

- `POST /mcp` ‚ÄĒ 19 X tools (see ¬ß3.3 `x/mcp.ts`). Client setup: `claude mcp add --transport http stratus https://<host>/mcp --header "Authorization: Bearer $STRATUS_TOKEN"`.
- `.claude/skills/stratus` ‚ÄĒ drives the HTTP API from Claude Code (scheduling scripts `md_to_schedule.ts` with the cadence ladders 3/day `[9,13,18]`, 4/day `[8,12,16,20]`; always jitter minutes).

## 7. Patterns & conventions (name these in plans; point implementers at the exemplar file)

**Money/API discipline**
1. **One place to call X / Grok / images**: `xFetch` / `askGrok` / `generateImages`. Never raw fetch.
2. **Retire-before-snapshot** (dailyMetrics): a billed read must be unrepeatable ‚ÄĒ take the row out of the candidate set in a committed txn BEFORE the read/write that follows. At-most-once, never double-charge.
3. **Claim-before-call** (publisher, winner re-read): commit the state flip before the irreversible external call.
4. **Refuse-before-spend**: validation ‚Üí band gate ‚Üí grounding checks ‚Üí THEN the paid call (replies.ts, icebreakers.ts, images.ts hard budget).
5. **`max_results` clamps** on every paginate wrapper (endpoints.ts pattern).
6. **costHint** when the URL can't price itself; `console.warn` on $0-priced billed calls.

**Data discipline**
7. **Deterministic event ids** `type:ref_table:ref_id` + INSERT OR IGNORE ‚ÄĒ backfill, live hooks, and DOM ingest share one idempotent id space (people/store.ts, launch.ts). **Bounded-re-log variant (sightings.ts, NT.2 engagements.ts):** when no ref resolves, bucket the id by UTC day (`‚Ä¶:<YYYY-MM-DD>`) instead of falling back to a random uuid ‚ÄĒ a re-scroll then collapses into one event/day/handle/kind rather than flooding the timeline. A once-ever fact (a follow) drops the date too.
8. **Best-effort side writes**: `safeLogPersonEvents`, `persistRadarDrafts`, `consumeIdeaSafe` ‚ÄĒ a hook failure never fails the paying path.
9. **Fill-only vs overwrite upserts**: hover/launch glimpses fill-only; profile scrapes overwrite (people/store.ts).
10. **Status ratchets**: stages only auto-promote; radar drafts ready‚Üíclicked‚Üíexpired; mentions never regress implicitly.
11. **null = unknown, never "no"** (`has_media`, `pinned_tweet_id`); bucket null separately in aggregations.
12. **No derived-state tables** when a read-time regroup works (conversations C2, momentum C5).
13. **Sync SQLite**: txns take sync callbacks (`.all()/.get()/.run()`, no await inside); never bind a JS `Date` in raw `sql` (use `.getTime()`); token refresh critical section = in-process mutex.
13a. **Millisecond ties break ordering logic**: writes are sub-millisecond here, so any column an ordering/recency rule reads (`created_at` insertion order, `last_used_at` anti-repeat) must be stamped **monotonically past the row set's current max**, not from `Date.now()` alone. Exemplars both in `replyLists.ts`: items `createdAt` (RL.2), `/use` `lastUsedAt` (RL.3 ‚ÄĒ measured: 241/500 uses shared a millisecond and 4 immediate repeats slipped through without it).
- **API checkpoint columns are never written from the page (C7 launch.ts, C10 notifications)**: `mentions`'s max tweet_id IS the since_id checkpoint, so a DOM-scraped id would skip every unseen mention ‚ÄĒ page surfaces READ mention rows for context and route their own writes into `person_events` instead; freshness gaps close via a human-clicked capped refresh, never an auto-pull.

- **Ambient ingest = free-text discriminator + server-owned parent row + lazy prune (HV.1 `POST /harvest/passive`)**: a high-volume DOM feed reuses the existing table instead of forking one ‚ÄĒ discriminated by a `mode` value the client-facing create route still rejects, hung off one server-found-or-created per-UTC-day run, retention pruned on the ingest path rather than by a new worker (¬ß7.12 spirit). Before opening the tap, check that **every existing reader already filters on that discriminator**. **The client half (HV.2)** is the flushSightings transport with one extra rule: the ambient flush is **warn-and-drop, never retried** (a lost sighting is a missing point on a curve, not a lost user action), its resend throttle mirrors the server's recapture window so the wire carries no row the server would only skip, and the expensive DOM read sits BEHIND the throttle check ‚ÄĒ a scan-loop hook runs on every mutation burst, so gate order is the performance contract.

**Prompt discipline**
14. **Byte-sync prompts**: `.md` ‚ÜĒ TS literal asserted by test; regenerate the literal when editing the .md.
15. **Variable tail**: ALL per-call content ({{TWEET_CONTEXT}}, {{PILLARS}}, relationship, guidance, idea) after the stable cacheable instruction prefix; `prompt_cache_key` set.
16. **Server-stamped fields**: `relationship`/`guidance`/gate signals are stamped server-side, never parsed from clients; persist exactly what the model saw in `contextSnapshot`.
17. **Structured outputs** via `text.format` json_schema on `/v1/responses` (`response_format` 400s there).
18. **No fabrication**: Grok may narrate only supplied FACTS; grounding blocks travel back in responses.
- **Niche persona substitution (N.3/N.4)**: `{{PERSONA}}`/`{{BELIEFS}}` (post) and `{{REPLY_PERSONA}}` (reply, single + batch) substitute IN PLACE (deliberate ¬ß7.15 deviation ‚ÄĒ constant per niche ‚áí prefix byte-stable per niche); all niche fields are server-stamped from `loadActiveNicheSafe()` (never client-parsed) and cache keys carry `:slug:updatedAtMs` to bust on edits. The reply routes also stamp `contextSnapshot.niche={slug}` (single path only ‚ÄĒ batch has no DB row) and load the niche AFTER the band gate. Seed-niche output is bit-for-bit identical to pre-extraction (equivalence tests in `src/test.test.ts` with independent fixtures ‚ÄĒ never re-read the .md, it holds the tokens now). **N.5 (doctrine):** the 5 REPLY-GUIDE knobs (reply target min/max, week reply %, target band min/max √ó) are owned by `niches.doctrine`; consumers call `loadDoctrine()` (never throws, resolves over `DEFAULT_DOCTRINE`) ‚ÄĒ `targetBand`'s new 2nd arg defaults to `{minX:2,maxX:10}` so untouched call sites/tests stay green (regression), and null doctrine = today's numbers. Doctrine is method-configuration, NOT a stat ‚ÄĒ no gates touched (¬ß7.19). **N.6 (ownership):** `content_pillars.niche` + `channels.niche` (nullable, backfilled `builder`) make pillars/channels owned by a niche; all list/active reads scope by `ownedByNiche(activeSlug)` = `niche = active.slug OR niche IS NULL` (legacy tolerance ‚ÄĒ identity until a 2nd niche exists), POSTs stamp the active slug, the channel `:slug` room 404s cross-niche, and `getActivePillars()` returns `[]` for a non-`builder` niche with no pillars ‚Üí the drafter refuses `409 no_pillars_for_niche` before any Grok spend (zero builder-pillar leakage into another niche's drafts). Last-active pillar 409 is now per-niche. PATCH/DELETE stay slug-addressed (admin can still edit another niche's rows). **AI.3 (prompt registry):** editable prompts live as OVERRIDE ROWS in `prompt_overrides` ‚ÄĒ row absent = shipped default, restore = DELETE, `customized` is structural row-presence (never a diff). Call sites load `loadPromptSafe(key)` and thread the body into the builders (`buildGrokInput` opts `template?` / `BuildPostDraftOptions.template?`; a per-request `systemPromptOverride` beats the DB override ‚ÄĒ explicit > DB > code-default); cache keys = registry sha-8 + the niche `:slug:updatedAtMs` suffix (both dimensions vary the rendered prefix). `validatePromptBody` guards edits: `required` placeholders must survive, the niche persona placeholders are `optional` (token-tolerant ‚ÄĒ an override hardcoding its persona is sanctioned, D29d), unknown tokens warn. A new editable prompt = one `PROMPT_SPECS` entry + a call-site wire (AI.4 adds the editor routes; AI.5/AI.6 migrated the 7 existing prompts, AI.7/AI.8/AI.9 added the three new-surface prompts thread/rewrite/ideas, RL.4 appended `reply-list` ‚ÄĒ **11 keys**). Registry defaults MUST come from PURE modules ‚ÄĒ a route-file import cycles (AI.5's `voice/extractPrompt.ts` move exists for exactly that; digest.ts/icebreakers.ts were already pure enough). (Unnumbered ‚ÄĒ the numbered `¬ß7.N` refs are load-bearing; don't renumber.)

**Stats discipline**
19. **Gates**: playbook cells + all lifts n‚Č•20/side (`DEFAULT_MIN_CELL_N`, **HV.5**: the timeline funnel gates on its `seen` DENOMINATOR, not on measured outcomes ‚ÄĒ `rate` null below it); angle preference ‚Č•3 measured; best-times top n‚Č•3; BAND recalibration ‚Č•100 and manual-only. Below gate ‚Üí `sufficient:false`/null, never a confident number.

**Routing/wiring traps**
20. **Static path before `:param`** (followups+fans and rankmap before `/people/:handle`) ‚ÄĒ check on every new people-adjacent route.
21. **Public-by-design routes** (`/healthz`, `/explorer`) mount at root outside the `/x/*` guard.
22. **LLM-gated mount vs runtime 503** (AI.6 ‚ÄĒ was Grok-gated): user-facing-always routes mount always + check `llmConfigured()` (EITHER provider) at runtime ‚Üí 503; pure LLM routes (`replies`/`drafter`/`voiceExtract`) refuse to mount unless `llmConfigured()`. `askLLM` still enforces the RESOLVED provider's key per request (503 `llm_not_configured`) ‚ÄĒ the mount/pre-flight gate is only "is ANY provider available". `images` stays `XAI_API_KEY`-only (Decision 6). The pre-flight 503 strings on pillars-draft/extract-winners/icebreaker stay `grok_not_configured` (stable extension matchers); only digest's degrade field renamed to `llm_not_configured`.
23. **Worker-owned statuses**: PATCH/DELETE 409 on `publishing`/`posted`.

**Extension**
24. **Background = single session-storage writer**; content/panel talk via messages, never write directly.
25. **One transport**: all HTTP through `ApiRequest`; blobs via `ApiRequest.binary`.
26. **Content script is an IIFE**: no module imports at runtime; shared code gets inlined ‚ÄĒ heavy deps stay out.
27. **Shims for shared server modules** (replyBand, channelSuggest) ‚ÄĒ never fork logic between server and page.
28. **Posting is always manual paste** ‚ÄĒ OAuth 1.0a media wall + reply policy; nothing auto-posts to others, MCP can only create `draft` rows.
- **Design tokens (UI.8)**: the panel's `styles.css` `:root` carries the `--strat-*` token set (from `Stratus Design System/tokens/*.css`) + `--x-*` companion tokens + legacy short aliases. New UI references `--strat-*` directly; tinted fills use the exact fill tokens or `color-mix(in srgb, var(--strat-*) N%, transparent)`; **no color literal lives outside `:root`**. **UI.9** made it theme-aware: `:root[data-theme='light']` redefines only the base `--strat-*` tokens (the whole sheet re-tints via the aliases), `main.tsx` stamps `data-theme`/`data-density`/`data-scale` on `<html>` from the local `theme`/`density`/`uiScale` settings (`system` resolved via `matchMedia` + listener). Appearance is panel-local (chrome.storage), never server-synced; content-script overlays and the Studio canvas are exempt (they follow X / the brand kit). (Unnumbered ‚ÄĒ the numbered `¬ß7.N` refs are load-bearing across CLAUDE.md/plans; don't renumber.)
- **Settings platform (UI.1)**: server-side tunable knobs live in `app_settings` (override rows) + the typed `src/x/settings/registry.ts` catalog. Discipline: **only routes/workers read the store** via the bound `getSetting`; **pure modules stay pure** and take an opts object defaulted to today's constant (`computeQuests(rows, opts = QUEST_DEFAULTS)`) ‚ÄĒ so every existing pure test stays valid and the store is mockable. Registry floors/ceilings are the money/policy guard (an MCP agent editing via `x_update_setting` hits the same wall). The shared store (`src/settings/store.ts`) never imports `src/x/*` ‚ÄĒ the registry is passed in. (Unnumbered ‚ÄĒ see the `don't renumber` note above.)
- **UI primitives (UI.10, D7 standing)**: every NEW panel surface from Wave 1 on composes `src/sidepanel/ui/` primitives (Section/EmptyState/SubTabs/SettingRow/Slider/GearPopover) + `--strat-*` tokens ‚ÄĒ no bespoke `<h3>`/muted-`<p>`/hand-rolled controls. Primitives are pure presentation (className + tokens, no state libs, no API calls); the settings PATCH lives in `settingsClient.ts`, and the panel renders knobs from `GET /x/settings` (extension never imports the server registry). Wave-5 polish (UI.12‚Äď16) migrates the pre-masterplan tabs onto them. (Unnumbered ‚ÄĒ see the `don't renumber` note above.)

**Process**
29. **Docs sync in the same commit**: `docs/PHASE-HISTORY.md` phase entry (NOT CLAUDE.md ‚ÄĒ slimmed 2026-07-23; CLAUDE.md changes only when a guardrail changes), the relevant plan doc (PLAN/CIRCLES/SURFACES), the matching `docs/<tab>.md`, and THIS codemap.
30. **Smoke script per feature**: rerunnable, $0 default, `--live` for the one paid verification, cleans up after itself.
31. **No obvious comments; comments explain why** (cost trade-off, policy quirk, race). No emojis.
32. **Never write a raw control char into source ‚ÄĒ use the escape** (RL.7): `src/x/playbook.ts` held two literal NUL bytes as a composite-key sentinel, which made `file` report it as `data` and made **every `grep` over it silently return nothing** (`grep -a` was the only way to find `classifyReplyOrigin`). Fixed to `'\0'`; identical at runtime, greppable again. One-command audit: `for f in $(git ls-files '*.ts'); do file $f | grep -q ': data' && echo $f; done`.

## 8. Cost & policy invariants (condensed ‚ÄĒ full text in CLAUDE.md)

- URL in post text = **$0.20 vs $0.015** (13x). `createPost` guard; links go in first reply ($0.030 total).
- **Feb 2026**: programmatic replies to non-self tweets blocked on self-serve (except when @-mentioned ‚ÄĒ unverified, `MENTION_API_REPLIES=false`). Quote-of-others blocked. Self-reply/self-quote OK (self-quote verified via `verifiedSelfQuote`).
- Token rotation: persist new refresh token BEFORE returning access token.
- Owned reads $0.001; other-user reads $0.005; third-party user lookup $0.010; post $0.015; delete $0.010.
- Media upload requires OAuth 1.0a ‚ÄĒ **not supported**; Studio images are manual paste.
- Budgets: X soft $0.15/day (log), xAI images hard $0.50/day (429).
- Out of scope v1: multi-tenant, follower sync, media upload, Chrome Web Store, idempotency drafts, per-tier caps.

## 9. Tests & verification map

- `bun test` runs with `SQLITE_PATH=:memory:` (one shared in-memory DB across route suites ‚ÄĒ seed carefully, clean up; some suites assert exact medians over shared data).
- Pure suites live next to their module (`*.test.ts`); route suites hit the Hono `app` via `app.request` over the in-memory DB; pre-DB guards in `src/app.test.ts`.
- Extension tests: bun:test on shared modules + studio (`templates.test.ts` (S5.6 code-card block; S5.7 thread-cover/list-card/parseListItems blocks; S5.8 chart growth/heatmap blocks), `chartData.test.ts` (S5.8 growthSeries + heatmapCells gate/normalization), `codeTokens.test.ts` (S5.6 tokenizer splits + `MONO_ADVANCE`), `milestones.test.ts` (S5.5 crossing logic), `brandKit.test.ts`, `mascot.test.ts`, `compose.test.ts`); DOM fixtures via happy-dom (earlyReplies); `sidepanel/storage.test.ts` mocks `chrome.storage.local` for the settings round-trip + `resolveTheme` (UI.9); **RU.6** `shared/messages.test.ts` (message-guard suite ‚ÄĒ `isRadarConfirm`; **RU.7** +`isRadarVariantsGet`/`isRadarVariantPasted`); **RU.7** `shared/variantChips.test.ts` (`variantChipPreview` truncation/whitespace/ellipsis-trim + `isReplyVariants` shape/empty/loose-angle); **AX.4** `shared/tweetContext.test.ts` (hand-built dossier JSON fixture, not happy-dom ‚ÄĒ rich happy path exact numbers / thin person / angle gate 2-vs-3 + split-cell total / alreadyReplied hit+miss+unlinked / momentum single-point + same-day clamp / open-loop filtering + order / outcome cap).
- `extension/src/shared/notifications.test.ts` (**NT.1**): happy-dom fixtures for the notification cell ‚ÄĒ the four kinds, aggregated/deduped/lowercased handles, the `unknown` + bad-handle skips, ro keyword fallback (apreciat/redistribuit/urmńÉre), icon-beats-misleading-header, skeleton cell, ellipsis strip (both `‚Ä¶` and `...`), longest-block target pick, follow-with-bio ‚Üí null, non-notification element ‚Üí null. **The fixtures build their glyphs FROM the exported icon-prefix constants**, so correcting a prefix after the live browser walk needs no test edit.
- `src/x/people/{stage,engagements}.test.ts` (**NT.2**): `stage` gained a C10 block ‚ÄĒ each engagement type is in `PERSON_EVENT_TYPES` but in neither exported stage set and alone computes `stranger` (that last assertion is what covers the unexported `NOTICED_TYPES`), 50 likes + a repost + a follow is still `stranger`, and a `mutual` history plus engagement stays `mutual`. `engagements` ‚ÄĒ pure dedupe/id/summary/prefix-match matrices, then ingest over the shared in-memory DB: person created `source='notification'` + stage `stranger`, resolved-target vs day-bucket vs follow ids, the same batch twice ‚Üí `events: 0`, next-day re-log ‚Üí +1 (follow never repeats), invalid handle skipped, fill-only upsert, `mutual` unmoved with `lastInboundAt` untouched. **Seeded `posts_published` rows carry a January `postedAt` and no metrics snapshot** so they sit outside every window/measured aggregation other suites assert over, and cleanup runs inline + in `afterAll`. **NT.3** appended the route suite to the same file (sightings' colocation precedent ‚ÄĒ `POST /x/people/sightings` lives in `people/sightings.test.ts`, not `routes/people.test.ts`): batch round-trip + normalized person + re-post logs nothing, invalid handle ‚Üí `skipped:1` not fatal, two follow cells with different `targetText` collapse to `processed:1` (the route's follow-null coercion), and the full validation matrix ending in "nothing was written" (every guard fires pre-DB).
- `src/openrouter/client.test.ts` (**AI.1**): pure ‚ÄĒ an injected `fetchImpl` records the request, no network. Covers OpenAI-shape mapping (jsonSchema‚Üíresponse_format, effort 'none' omitted, `usage.include`/`provider.require_parameters` always), cost off `usage.cost` (+ $0/warn when missing), retry classification (429/503 retry via `retry-after:0`, 400 throws once), numeric-error-code coercion, and the soft budget watchdog. Cleans up its `platform='openrouter'` `cost_events` rows in `afterAll`; sets a dummy key + high budget in `beforeEach` (watchdog test uses its own low budget).
- `src/llm/{settings,ask,routes}.test.ts` (**AI.2**): `settings` ‚ÄĒ defaults on empty DB, save/merge round-trip, garbage-row sanitize, `parseAiPatch` per-field validation. `ask` ‚ÄĒ runtime gates, `resolveProvider` precedence, the no-silent-fallback `LlmNotConfiguredError` (both provider directions), and the openrouter dispatch via an injected `fetchImpl` (endpoint + response_format mapping + opts>settings>defaults merge). `routes` ‚ÄĒ bare-Hono `app.request`: GET/PATCH settings, per-field 400s, 409 `provider_not_configured`, models 503. **Env-key discipline:** unset = `process.env.X = ''` (falsy, NOT `delete` ‚ÄĒ biome `noDelete`; AI.1 pattern), saved/restored per test; all three clean up their `app_settings` `'ai'` row (+ ask cleans openrouter `cost_events`).
- `src/x/prompts/registry.test.ts` (**AI.3**): loadPrompt default-fallback + override-wins over the shared in-memory DB (afterEach deletes all `prompt_overrides` rows ‚ÄĒ other suites render prompts and must see defaults), sha cache-key stability/distinctness, `validatePromptBody` matrices (missing required / optional-droppable niche placeholders / unknown-token dedup), `renderPrompt` $-safety, and the builders' `template` param (marker template renders; per-request override beats the DB template; `{{REPLY_PERSONA}}` still substitutes in a custom template; explicit default template byte-identical to omitting it).
- `src/x/routes/prompts.test.ts` (**AI.4**): bare-Hono `app.request` over the shared in-memory DB (afterEach+afterAll wipe `prompt_overrides` ‚ÄĒ other prompt-rendering suites must see defaults) ‚ÄĒ GET list uncustomized, GET default body, PATCH missing-placeholder 400 + `missing`, valid PATCH ‚Üí customized + `unknownPlaceholders` + `loadPrompt` reflects it + other key untouched, 32KB‚Üí413, empty/absent body 400, reset scoping, restore-defaults `{restored:n}` + list all-uncustomized, unknown-key 404 (GET/PATCH/reset), and the done-when chain (override ‚Üí `loadPrompt` reflects ‚Üí restore reverts). The bearer 401 is NOT duplicated (shared `/x` middleware, covered by app.test/mcp.test ‚ÄĒ niche.test discipline).
- `src/x/replyLists/engine.test.ts` (**RL.1**): stubbed-rng matrices (render degradation, pick exclusion windows at n=2/3/6, humanizer step order + strict thresholds + the fixed 10-draw contract via a `counted` rng) plus seeded `mulberry32` sweeps for the statistical promises ‚ÄĒ 200 runs asserting protected spans are never mutated and the typo rate tracks the configured chance (0 ‚Üí none, 5% ‚Üí single digits). No DB, no `Math.random`.
- `src/x/replyLists/generate.test.ts` (**RL.4**): pure ‚ÄĒ `buildListGenInput` tail placement (request + existing items after `## Rules`), count/empty-list placeholders, a registry override body as the base + default byte-identity, `$&`/`$'`/`` $` `` survival (split/join), and the no-persona-token assertion; `parseGeneratedItems` happy path, empty/over-280/non-string drops, casing+whitespace dedupe, count cap, malformed ‚Üí null vs a legal `[]`. No DB, no network.
- `src/x/routes/replyLists.test.ts` (**RL.2**): bare-Hono `app.request` over the shared in-memory DB ‚ÄĒ CRUD round-trip (trim/defaults, grouped counts, patch, delete‚Üí404), cascade (items gone after the list), replace-vs-append semantics (ids swapped, whole-set response, empty replace clears), item writes scoped to their list (right item + wrong list ‚Üí 404 on PATCH and DELETE), and the guard matrix (name bounds, humanizer null-clears/partial-parses/non-object-400s, item text 1..280 + the 100-cap boundary, bare-string items rejected, unknown-vs-malformed ids 404 vs 400, `empty_patch`). **RL.3** adds the `/use` describe: 10 sequential uses on a 5-item list (no back-to-back repeat, 10 `reply_list_uses` rows, `useCount` sums to 10), preview writes nothing, var fill + missing-var degradation, the use row's rendered text + normalized target, 409 on empty/all-disabled, and the guard matrix. Every text assertion runs on a list whose `humanizer` is all-zero-chance ‚ÄĒ the route calls `Math.random` for real, and the jitter itself is the engine suite's job. **RL.4** adds the `/generate` describe ‚ÄĒ guards only, nothing may reach an LLM: the 400 matrix (bad body/prompt/count 0¬∑31¬∑2.5/model/provider/uuid), a 404 for an unknown list *before* the call, and a both-keys-force-unset 503 `llm_not_configured` that also asserts the list stayed empty (proposal-only). Tracks every list it creates and deletes them in `afterAll` ‚ÄĒ **`reply_list_uses` rows must be deleted explicitly** (FK-free, so they don't cascade and would leak into RL.7's `canned` attribution).
- `src/x/{playbook,routes/playbook}.test.ts` (**RL.7**): the `canned` bucket. Pure ‚ÄĒ canned checked LAST (a posted draft that also text-matches counts `single`), a right-text/wrong-radar-target reply falls through to `canned`, empty bucket is a zero cell. Route ‚ÄĒ the `canned attribution (RL.7)` describe seeds a published reply, snapshots `batchVsSingle` BEFORE inserting the `reply_list_uses` row, then asserts the **delta** (canned +1, unattributed ‚ąí1) rather than absolutes: `reply_list_uses` is FK-free (D79i) so another suite can leave strays; the exact median is asserted only on a clean run.
- `src/x/routes/harvest.test.ts` (**HV.1**, the file's FIRST route suite ‚ÄĒ `parseIngestRow`/`matchUnlinkedDraft` unit tests stay in `src/test.test.ts`): bare-Hono `app.request` over the shared in-memory DB ‚ÄĒ pure `utcDayStart`, pre-DB 400s (`too_many_rows` at 101, indexed `invalid_row_tweet_id`) asserted to leave zero timeline runs behind, run created once then reused same-day, in-batch dupe + 30-min recapture ‚Üí `skippedRecent`, a row aged past the window re-captures into a 2-point series, the cap (`rowCount` forced to 1999 then **restored** ‚ÄĒ later tests in the file would otherwise be capped), and the prune sparing a same-age `posts`-mode run. **HV.4** added a LAST describe for `GET /harvest/affinity` (+5): its rows are seeded **directly** (the 30-min recapture gate makes a multi-day history unbuildable through the ingest) under **its own run created NOW with backdated rows**, so the 60-day prune can never take them; six seeded handles cover ranking (4 days > 3 days, sightings as tiebreak), the floor, the `people`/`voice_authors` join (incl. a retired person ‚Üí `stage:null, inRoster:true`), the window (a 40-day-old author absent at `days=30`, present at `days=90`), the clamps, the 400s, and a `mode='posts'` author proving the corpus never mixes. It must stay last ‚ÄĒ the ingest describe's first test asserts **zero** timeline runs exist. `afterAll` deletes every `mode='timeline'` run+rows plus the seeded keeper **and the seeded `people`/`voice_authors` rows** (shared in-memory DB).

Extension test files are typechecked by NEITHER tsconfig (root `include` stops at `src/`, `tsconfig.app.json` excludes `**/*.test.ts`) ‚ÄĒ only `bun run test` runs them.

the fill survives humanization because typos never touch a protected value) ‚Üí `preview:true` moves neither `use_count` nor the use rows ‚Üí empty list `409 no_enabled_items` ‚Üí `mode:'replace'` swaps the set (new ids, `source:'ai'`) ‚Üí **the Playbook `canned` delta**: snapshot `GET /x/playbook`, insert a `posts_published` reply whose text IS one use's `renderedText` + a `metrics_snapshots` row, re-GET and assert `canned.posted`/`canned.n` **+1** with `unattributed` unmoved (delta, never absolute ‚ÄĒ the FK-free use table may hold other rows) ‚Üí DELETE the list, asserting items cascaded and all 10 use rows survived. The live `contextSnapshot.niche.slug` proof rides a real reply-generate (D29b) ‚ÄĒ deliberately not in the $0 default.
- `smoke-notifications.ts` (**NT.7**): mounts followups+people in-process over the REAL DB (followups first ‚ÄĒ ¬ß7.20) and drives the C10 harvest end-to-end: one synthetic 4-engagement batch ‚Üí `{received:4, processed:4, skipped:0, events:4}`, the three id shapes asserted literally (resolved `their_like:notif:<h>:<tweetId>` via prefix match, day-bucket `their_repost:notif:<h>:<YYYY-MM-DD>`, `their_follow:notif:<h>`), fill-only proof (a pre-seeded enriched person keeps `source='mention'`+displayName while the fresh one is `source='notification'`), **identical re-POST ‚Üí `events: 0`**, both people still `stranger` with the engagements on the timeline, `/x/people/fans` showing `inboundCount:1 / engagementCount:3` for the fan while the likes-only lurker **never ranks** (decision 1, structurally), `kind:'other'` ‚Üí 400, then surgical cleanup verified by a 404. Handles are ‚Č§15 chars (else `normalizePersonHandle` skips them and every assertion goes vacuous) and the seeded own post is written **`retired: true`** so an aborted run can never leave a row the daily pass would bill.
- `smoke-passive-harvest.ts` (**HV.6**): mounts harvest + playbook in-process over the REAL DB and drives the whole HV phase ‚ÄĒ passive batch ‚Üí run (`timeline/timeline/passive`) + rows all `mode='timeline'` under the returned runId; immediate re-POST ‚Üí `skippedRecent:3`, same run (no per-POST fork); the same tweet twice in one batch ‚Üí 1 insert / 1 skip; a 101-row batch ‚Üí `400 too_many_rows` with the stored count unmoved (the guard is pre-DB); a seeded 61-day-old passive run + its row pruned by the next POST; `GET /harvest/affinity` returning the 4-distinct-day author (`avgViews`, `stage:null`, `inRoster:false`) while both one-day handles are floored by `minDays 3`; `GET /playbook` carrying `timelineFunnel` with `totalSeen ‚Č• 11` and an `'unknown'` cell of ‚Č•6 (the seeds deliberately carry no `tweetTime`). **Real-DB safety is the interesting part:** every row is 888-prefixed (no real snowflake starts there) and every seeded run carries an `hv6_*` handle, so cleanup's LIKE/inArray can never sweep a genuine passive run or hand harvest; today's pre-existing passive run is **kept** and its `row_count` recomputed from the survivors rather than restored from a remembered number. Cleanup is sync (bun:sqlite) and runs from `fail()` too. Reuse this shape for any smoke that writes into a table the user's live browsing also writes.
- Studio (S5) browser verification (ST.9, 2026-07-18): the deterministic-render discipline (S3) ‚ÄĒ a throwaway Bun-served harness bundles the real `compose`/`templates`/`registry` modules and renders every template onto a canvas in Chrome; confirms fonts/mascot/presets/pattern-determinism/Copy-PNG. Reusable pattern for future Studio visual QA; the harness entry is not committed.
- Gates before commit: `bun test` + `bun run typecheck` + `bun run lint`.
- Deploy: `./scripts/deploy.sh` (rsync, migrate ‚ÄĒ aborts restart on failure, `.git-sha` stamp, `curl -f /healthz`).

## 10. Recipes ‚ÄĒ where new things go

- **New API surface**: pure logic in `src/x/<domain>.ts` or `src/x/<domain>/` ‚Üí router in `src/x/routes/<name>.ts` ‚Üí mount in `src/x/index.ts` (mind order + Grok gating) ‚Üí route test + pure test ‚Üí smoke script ‚Üí docs sync. If MCP-worthy, add a curated tool in `src/x/mcp.ts` (in-process `app.request`).
- **New table/column**: `src/x/db/schema.ts` ‚Üí `bun run db:generate` ‚Üí inspect SQL for dropped seeds ‚Üí consumers. Column semantics: nullable + null=unknown when backfill is impossible.
- **New worker**: `src/x/workers/` ‚Üí register heartbeat + stop() in `startXWorkers` ‚Üí healthz staleness window. Prefer read-time computation over a new worker when $0-equivalent (¬ß7.12).
- **New extension surface**: component in `src/sidepanel/` ‚Üí wire in `App.tsx` ‚Üí API via `api.ts` ‚Üí shared pure logic in `src/shared/` or `extension/src/shared/` (bun-tested) ‚Üí `docs/<tab>-tab.md`. Content-script additions must stay IIFE-safe.
- **New prompt-affecting feature**: NEVER edit the template mid-file ‚ÄĒ inject at the variable tail; keep byte-sync tests green; stamp what the model saw into the draft's snapshot.
- **New measurement**: pure `build*` in `src/x/playbook.ts` (gated) ‚Üí loader in `routes/playbook.ts` ‚Üí Playbook tab section ‚Üí optionally digest facts.

## 11. Update log

- 2026-07-23 `7e66a22`+GR.1 ‚ÄĒ **GR.1** (the GR lane OPENS ‚ÄĒ following ledger schema + ingest/ratchet routes; xhigh, no deps, **$0**; 5 files: `src/x/db/schema.ts`, migration **`0019_messy_blue_shield`**, NEW `src/x/routes/following.ts` + NEW `src/x/routes/following.test.ts`, `src/x/index.ts`). Two tables (¬ß4) + `POST /following/runs|rows`, `GET /following`, `PATCH /following/:handle` (¬ß3.4). **The design turns on one asymmetry:** a handle's PRESENCE in any scrape is ground truth, but its ABSENCE only means something if the scroll reached the end of the list ‚ÄĒ so batches update what they see and nothing else, and only a run closed `done:true` reconciles. **Three judgement calls the plan text didn't pin (D99):** (a) a `confirmed`/`gone` row seen again is **revived to `active`** ‚ÄĒ without it a re-followed person is invisible to the queue forever ‚ÄĒ but `first_seen_at` is NOT reset (it is the only follow-age signal, and a bad reconcile must not erase it) and `unfollow_marked_at` is never cleared (it is churn history the 6h/24h budgets count); (b) a run that closed having seen **zero rows** gets `completed_at` but **`complete: false`**, so a broken selector can't conclude "I follow nobody" and mass-flip the ledger to `gone` ‚ÄĒ decision 9 generalized from cancelled runs to empty ones; (c) an **empty `rows` array is legal when `done:true`**, because a scrape whose row count lands on an exact batch boundary must still be able to close its run. `first_seen_at` fill-only + don't-erase-what-you-didn't-see on `displayName`/`listPosition`; `follows_back` is notNull and **required** in the payload (a build that can't read the badge must fail loudly, not mark the whole roster as non-reciprocating). `keep` moves no status ‚ÄĒ **GR.3's queue must filter kept rows out of the already-`queued` batch itself**. Suite 1176‚Üí**1190**. **Next: GR.2** (harvester following mode, deps GR.1‚úď+HV.2‚úď ‚ÄĒ takes the `extension/src/harvester.ts` lock) or **GR.3** (curation queue, dep GR.1‚úď ‚ÄĒ `GET /following/queue` above `:handle`, plus pure `src/x/connections.ts`).

- 2026-07-23 `c3f44d2` ‚ÄĒ **RL.3** (reply lists ‚ÄĒ `POST /reply-lists/:id/use`: anti-repeat pick + humanized render + stamp; deps RL.1‚úď+RL.2‚úď, high, $0, 2 files, +6 tests). The route is thin on purpose ‚ÄĒ the engine already owns every decision: load the list (for its normalized `humanizer`) and **all** its items (pickItem owns the enabled/var-availability rules, so the filtering lives in exactly one place), `pickItem(items, availableVarsFor(vars), Math.random)` ‚Üí **409 `no_enabled_items`** when nothing is usable (covers both an empty list and an all-disabled one), `composeReply(item.text, vars, resolveHumanizer(list.humanizer), Math.random)` ‚ÄĒ note the plan's `protectedValues = [vars.name, vars.handle]` argument doesn't exist: RL.1's `composeReply` derives the protected spans (name/first_name/handle) internally. Unless `preview:true`, ONE sync txn (¬ß7.13) stamps `lastUsedAt` + `use_count + 1` (via `sql\`${col} + 1\``, the dailyMetrics pollCount idiom) and inserts the `reply_list_uses` row. **The one thing worth carrying forward (D79):** `lastUsedAt` is stamped **monotonically past the list's current max**, not from `Date.now()` ‚ÄĒ the anti-repeat window only holds while the just-used item is STRICTLY the most recent, and uses land ~0.5ms apart. Measured with a throwaway 500-use stress: with the stamp, 0 duplicate `usedAt` values and 0 immediate repeats; without it, **241/500 uses shared a millisecond and 4 immediate repeats slipped through** ‚ÄĒ i.e. the plan's own 10-use done-when test would have been ~8%-flaky. Same trap RL.2 hit on item `createdAt`, now ¬ß7.13a. Smaller calls: `updatedAt` is NOT bumped on use (it means "the text was edited"); an `active:false` list is still usable (active is presentation state ‚ÄĒ the contract lists only 404/409, so no new error code was invented); a body-less POST is a legitimate no-target use while a body parsing to a non-object 400s; `targetHandle` is normalized the repo way (`@`-stripped, lowercased, `USERNAME_RE`) and 400s if malformed, since it's audit metadata that later joins people/voice rows. Tests: the 10-use no-repeat + full stamping walk, preview-writes-nothing, var fill + missing-var degradation ("Thank you, {name}!" ‚Üí "Thank you!" + `missingVars:['name']`), the use row's rendered text/target, 409 on empty and all-disabled, and the guard matrix ‚ÄĒ all on an all-zero-chance humanizer, because the route calls `Math.random` for real. `afterAll` now also deletes `reply_list_uses` (FK-free by design ‚ÄĒ they don't cascade and would leak into RL.7's `canned` bucket). Gates: `bun run test` **1073/0** (+6), typecheck clean, full-repo lint 0-error. **Next:** RL.4 (AI generator, dep RL.2‚úď, **D5** ‚ÄĒ `askLLM` + a registry key) or RL.5; the NT server lane (NT.1/NT.2/NT.4) stays parallel-ok.
- 2026-07-22 `9c0d97b` ‚ÄĒ **RL.2** (reply lists ‚ÄĒ schema + CRUD routes + mount; dep RL.1‚úď, high, $0, 5 files, +8 tests). **Three tables** (migration `0018_flimsy_captain_universe.sql`, DDL-only, 3 CREATE TABLEs + 2 indexes, **no seed** so the drizzle-dropped-INSERT trap doesn't apply; verified against a copy of the real `stratus.db`: 36 tables after, `content_pillars` seed intact, FK cascade live): `reply_lists` (uuid PK, name, description, `humanizer` JSON, active, sortOrder) ‚Üí `reply_list_items` (uuid PK, `list_id` FK **ON DELETE CASCADE**, template `text`, `enabled`, `source` manual|ai, **`last_used_at`/`use_count` ‚ÄĒ the anti-repeat state lives server-side (Decision 1), index `(list_id,last_used_at)` = exactly `pickItem`'s recency read**) ‚Üí `reply_list_uses` (uuid PK, listId/itemId/`rendered_text`/target/usedAt, index `(used_at)`) ‚ÄĒ **uses are deliberately FK-free**: they're the audit log AND the Playbook `canned` hook, so the history must outlive an edited-away item or a deleted list. **Routes** `src/x/routes/replyLists.ts` (pillars.ts validation idiom, ideas.ts uuid/404 idiom; always mounted next to `ideasRouter`, $0): collection GET carries `itemCount`/`enabledCount` from ONE grouped select; `POST /:id/items` takes `{mode:'append'|'replace', items:[{text}] ‚Č§100, source?}` and runs **one sync txn** (¬ß7.13 ‚ÄĒ `.run()`/`.all()` terminals) so a replace never leaves the list emptied-then-crashed, and **always answers with the list's whole current set** so both modes read alike; item PATCH/DELETE are scoped by `id` AND `listId` (right item, wrong list ‚Üí 404). **Two contract calls worth knowing:** (a) `humanizer` is stored NORMALIZED through the engine's `parseHumanizerConfig` ‚ÄĒ `null` clears to `DEFAULT_HUMANIZER`, a non-object 400s `invalid_humanizer`, a partially-bad object is lenient-parsed and accepted (D76a made this possible); RL.3's `/use` therefore never re-validates. (b) item `createdAt` is stamped explicitly per row, starting past the list's current max, because a batch insert shares one `unixepoch()` millisecond and an append landing in the same ms as the previous batch would tie ‚ÄĒ insertion order is what the panel and the AI preview render. `MAX_REPLY_LENGTH` (280) is imported from the engine, not re-declared. Tests: CRUD round-trip, cascade, replace-vs-append, list-scoped item writes, and the guard matrix; every created list is deleted in `afterAll` (shared in-memory DB). - 2026-07-22 `ffbdb3f` ‚ÄĒ **RL.1** (reply lists ‚ÄĒ pure engine: render, anti-repeat pick, humanize; dep none, **xhigh**, $0, 2 new files, +39 tests). New `src/x/replyLists/engine.ts` (+`.test.ts`) ‚ÄĒ the whole feature's decision-making, before any table exists. **(a) `renderTemplate`** fills `{name}`/`{first_name}`/`{handle}` (name emoji/flag/ZWJ-stripped, handle `@`-stripped, first_name = first token); a var the target can't fill is removed **with exactly one adjacent separator** ‚ÄĒ the leading `", "`/`" "` when there is one, else the trailing one ‚ÄĒ so "Thank you, {name}!" degrades to "Thank you!" and never "Thank you, !"; a `tidy` pass collapses horizontal runs, pulls spaces off punctuation and drops a dangling trailing comma; unknown `{foo}` is intentional text, left verbatim; every unfilled var is reported in `missingVars` (never blocks the use, Decision 7). **(b) `pickItem`** ‚ÄĒ enabled only; items whose template needs an unavailable var are deprioritized (used only when nothing else remains ‚ÄĒ deprioritization outranks recency, so a var-free item repeats rather than blocking); then the `min(n-1, floor(n/2))` most-recently-used are excluded (`lastUsedAt` null = never used = most eligible; stable sort, input order preserved in the eligible set) and the pick is **uniform among the rest** ‚ÄĒ pure LRU cycling is itself a detectable pattern, so randomness inside the eligible half is the point. n‚Č•2 can never repeat the last-used item; n=1 repeats by necessity; n=0 ‚Üí null. Generic over `PickableItem` so RL.3 gets its row type back. **(c) `humanize`** ‚ÄĒ independent rolls in fixed order (prefix .25 ‚Üí suffix .20 ‚Üí lowercase .15 ‚Üí drop-period .10 ‚Üí typo .05), each skipped rather than truncated when it would clear `MAX_REPLY_LENGTH` (280). **`HUMANIZE_DRAWS`=10 rng draws are taken UP FRONT, every call, whether or not a step fires** ‚ÄĒ so a stubbed sequence maps to steps by position (0 prefix chance ¬∑ 1 prefix pick ¬∑ 2 suffix chance ¬∑ 3 suffix pick ¬∑ 4 lowercase ¬∑ 5 drop-period ¬∑ 6 typo chance ¬∑ 7 typo word ¬∑ 8 typo kind ¬∑ 9 typo position). The suffix joins with `" "` after terminal punctuation, else `", "`; drop-period leaves an ellipsis intact (`[^.]\.$`); lowercase targets the first letter of the item's own text (a `bodyStart` offset, so an applied prefix doesn't shield it) and skips a protected/`@`/`#` first word; the typo picks one of drop/swap/neighbor(QWERTY row)/double-space on a ‚Č•4-letter all-letter word that is **not** a mention, hashtag, link-ish token, or inside/containing a protected value ‚ÄĒ names and handles are never mangled (Decision 5). `applied: string[]` names what fired (`['prefix','typo:swap']`). **(d) `parseHumanizerConfig`** is the brandKit lenient parse (unknown fields ignored, bad fields fall back one by one, an explicitly empty pool honored) but returns **null ONLY when the value isn't an object** ‚ÄĒ the one deliberate contract addition beyond the plan text, because RL.2's CRUD needs to 400 `invalid_humanizer` while still storing a partial one; `resolveHumanizer(raw)` is the `?? DEFAULT_HUMANIZER` form the RL.3 `/use` path wants. `composeReply` = render ‚Üí humanize with the target's own name/first-name/handle as protected spans. Tests: stubbed-rng matrices for all three plus seeded `mulberry32` sweeps (200 runs: protected span intact every time, typo rate 0 at chance 0 and single-digit at 5%, links/mentions never mutated). Gates: `bun run test` **1059/0** (+39), typecheck clean, changed-file lint 0-error (the emoji class had to become an **alternation** ‚ÄĒ biome `noMisleadingCharacterClass` forbids a ZWJ inside `[...]`). **D75** (AX.7 sha reconciliation `00ec8a8`‚Üí`83f8c4d`, orphan GC'd; 3 out-of-skill commits landed after it ‚ÄĒ `912a9cb`/`1b2a474`/`2ffca50`, all `.md`/CSV plans+evals, no source touched, ledger no drift).
